# cs.SE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [To Diff or Not to Diff? Structure-Aware and Adaptive Output Formats for Efficient LLM-based Code Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27296v1)
*Wei Cheng,Yongchang Cao,Chen Shen,Binhua Li,Jue Chen,Yongbin Li,Wei Hu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出结构感知的差异格式和自适应编辑策略AdaEdit，使LLM在代码编辑中保持准确性的同时降低延迟和成本超过30%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全代码生成范式在LLM用于代码编辑时存在效率瓶颈，导致交互式编码助手延迟高、成本大；现有方法忽视编辑格式对生成的自然性和效率的影响。

Method: 设计BlockDiff和FuncDiff两种结构感知差异格式，将代码变化表示为语法连贯单元的块级重写；提出AdaEdit策略，训练LLM动态选择最令牌高效的格式（差异格式或全代码）。

Result: AdaEdit配合结构感知差异格式在长代码编辑任务上完全匹配全代码生成的准确性，同时降低延迟和成本超过30%。

Conclusion: 通过引入结构感知的差异格式和自适应编辑策略，可以在不牺牲准确性的前提下显著提升LLM代码编辑的效率，为交互式编码助手提供更实用的方案。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地用于代码编辑，然而普遍的全代码生成范式存在严重的效率瓶颈，给需要低延迟和低成本的交互式编码助手带来了挑战。尽管主要关注扩展模型能力，但编辑格式本身在模型训练中很大程度上被忽视了。本文首先对传统差异格式进行了系统研究，揭示了脆弱的偏移量和碎片化的块使得生成对LLM来说非常不自然。为解决这个问题，我们引入了BlockDiff和FuncDiff，两种结构感知的差异格式，将变化表示为语法连贯单元（如控制结构和函数）的块级重写。此外，我们提出了AdaEdit，一种通用的自适应编辑策略，训练LLM在给定的差异格式和全代码之间动态选择最令牌高效的格式。大量实验表明，AdaEdit与结构感知的差异格式配对，在全代码生成的准确性上持续匹配，同时在长代码编辑任务上将延迟和成本均降低超过30%。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used for code editing, yet the prevalent full-code generation paradigm suffers from severe efficiency bottlenecks, posing challenges for interactive coding assistants that demand low latency and cost. Despite the predominant focus on scaling model capabilities, the edit format itself has been largely overlooked in model training. In this paper, we begin with a systematic study of conventional diff formats and reveal that fragile offsets and fragmented hunks make generation highly unnatural for LLMs. To address it, we introduce BlockDiff and FuncDiff, two structure-aware diff formats that represent changes as block-level rewrites of syntactically coherent units such as control structures and functions. Furthermore, we propose AdaEdit, a general adaptive edit strategy that trains LLMs to dynamically choose the most token-efficient format between a given diff format and full code. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AdaEdit paired with structure-aware diff formats consistently matches the accuracy of full-code generation, while reducing both latency and cost by over 30% on long-code editing tasks.

</details>


### [2] [Pragmos: A Process Agentic Modeling System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27311v1)
*Pedro-Aarón Hernández-Ávalos,Luciano García-Bañuelos*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种结合LLM和专用工具的混合方法，通过交互式、迭代的对话过程进行过程建模，并实现原型系统Pragmos。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过程建模复杂，黑盒解决方案不可行，需要透明且可解释的交互式建模方法。

Method: 将建模任务分解为小步骤，每个步骤产生中间工件并记录决策原理，逐步揭示行为关系，并用专用工具补充LLM的推理不足。

Result: 提出了Pragmos原型系统，展示LLM与人类专家协作进行结构化过程建模。

Conclusion: 混合方法能够生成健全、可理解的模型，通过透明步骤演化，为LLM辅助过程建模提供了新思路。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的出现显著改变了软件工程中的各种任务。在业务流程管理领域，LLM 目前正被探索作为直接从文本描述中推导过程模型的工具。现有方法包括聊天机器人驱动的系统，协助进行迭代的、基于文本的建模，以及完全自动化的端到端建模助手。然而，我们认为过程建模本质上是复杂的，无法通过黑盒解决方案有效解决。相反，我们将建模设想为一种开放式的对话活动，最好通过涉及人类和 LLM 的交互式迭代过程来支持。在我们的方法中，建模任务被分解为更小的、可管理的步骤。每个步骤产生中间工件，并明确记录每个建模决策背后的原理。在此过程中，我们逐步揭示简单的行为关系，这些关系指导模型的构建。鉴于当前 LLM 在推理复杂依赖关系方面的局限性，我们使用该领域开发的专门工具来补充它们，以基于行为关系结构化过程模型。这种混合方法能够生成既健全又易于理解的模型，这些模型通过透明且可解释的步骤演化。在本文中，我们介绍了我们的研究议程，并提出了 Pragmos，一个实现这一愿景的原型系统。Pragmos 展示了 LLM 如何与人类用户（作为领域专家和建模专家）协作，通过结构化和可解释的工作流共同创建不断演进的过程模型。

Original abstract: The advent of Large Language Models (LLMs) has significantly transformed tasks across Software Engineering. In the context of Business Process Management, LLMs are now being explored as tools to derive process models directly from textual descriptions. Existing approaches range from chatbot-driven systems that assist with iterative, text-based modeling to fully automated end-to-end modeling assistants. However, we argue that process modeling is inherently complex and cannot be effectively addressed through black-box solutions. Instead, we envision modeling as an open-ended conversational activity, best supported by an interactive, iterative process involving both humans and LLM. In our approach, the modeling task is decomposed into smaller, manageable steps. Each step results in intermediate artifacts and explicitly documents the rationale behind each modeling decision. During this process, we incrementally uncover simple behavioral relations that guide the construction of the model. Given the current limitations of LLMs in reasoning about complex dependencies, we complement them with specialized tools developed in the field to structure process models based on behavioral relations. This hybrid approach enables the generation of sound, yet comprehensible models that evolve through transparent and explainable steps. In this paper, we present our research agenda and introduce Pragmos, a prototype system that operationalizes this vision. Pragmos demonstrates how LLMs can collaborate with human users as both domain and modeling experts to co-create evolving process models through a structured and explainable workflow.

</details>


### [3] [One Size Fits All? An Empirical Comparison of ADR Templates regarding Comprehension, Usability, and Ease of Adoption](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27333v1)
*Fernando Nogueira,Nabson Silva,Tayana Conte*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文比较了五种ADR模板，发现Nygard模板在总体得分上优于MADR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏比较不同ADR模板的实证证据，需要确定最佳模板以支持理解性、可用性和易于采用。

Method: 使用DESMET FA方法进行两步评估：专家初步筛选和受控实验。

Result: 专家筛选出Nygard和MADR；实验显示Nygard总体得分更高，定性分析揭示了模板偏好因素。

Conclusion: 提供了基于证据的ADR模板选择策略，帮助根据项目约束选择模板以减少文档开销和增加知识保留。

中文摘要：背景：记录架构设计决策（ADDs）是软件生命周期中的一个关键因素，对于高效的系统维护、开发人员入职和防止知识蒸发至关重要。尽管已经提出了各种架构决策记录（ADRs）的模板，但缺乏比较它们的实证证据。目标：为了解决这一空白，本文旨在确定哪种ADR模板最能支持理解性、可用性和易于采用：Tyree/Akerman的模板、Nygard的ADR、arc42、Y语句和MADR。方法：我们使用DESMET FA方法对这些模板进行了两步评估。首先，两位主要作者基于其软件架构专业知识，通过DESMET FA评估了五个模板。然后将表现最好的两个模板作为处理因素，在一项由本科生参与的受控实验中使用。结果：在专家初步筛选后，表现最好的模板是Nygard和MADR。在随后的受控实验中，Nygard的模板在总体得分上优于MADR。对参与者反馈的定性分析揭示了影响模板偏好的因素。研究结果表明，Nygard支持简洁客观的文档，而MADR有助于结构细节和特定的架构需求。结论：本文通过提供模板之间的比较，为ADR模板的采用提供了基于证据的策略。研究结果提供了一个决策指南，帮助从业者和研究人员根据项目约束选择ADR模板，旨在最小化文档开销并增加架构知识保留。

Original abstract: Context: Documenting Architectural Design Decisions (ADDs) is a critical factor in the software lifecycle, essential for efficient system maintenance, developer onboarding, and preventing knowledge vaporization. Although various templates for Architectural Decision Records (ADRs) have been proposed, there is a lack of empirical evidence comparing them.
  Goal: To address this gap, this paper aims to identify which ADR template best supports comprehension, usability, and ease of adoption: Tyree/Akerman's template, Nygard's ADR, arc42, Y-statements, and MADR.
  Method: We compared these templates using the DESMET FA method in a two-step evaluation. First, the two primary authors evaluated the five templates through the DESMET FA, based on their software architecture expertise. The two top-performing templates were then used as treatments in a controlled experiment conducted with undergraduate students.
  Results: In the preliminary screening by experts, the top-performing templates were those of Nygard and MADR. In the subsequent controlled experiment, Nygard's template outperformed MADR in terms of the Overall Score. Qualitative analysis of participant feedback revealed the factors influencing template preference. The findings indicate that Nygard supports concise and objective documentation, while MADR facilitates structural details and specific architectural requirements.
  Conclusion: This paper provides an evidence-based strategy for ADR template adoption by offering a comparison between them. The findings present a decision-making guide that assists practitioners and researchers in selecting ADR templates aligned with project constraints, aiming to minimize documentation overhead and increase architectural knowledge retention.

</details>


### [4] [ScaleBox: Enabling High-Fidelity and Scalable Code Verification for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27467v1)
*Jiasheng Zheng,Xin Zheng,Boxi Cao,Pengbo Wang,Zhengzhao Ma,Qiming Zhu,Jiazhen Jiang,Yaojie Lu,Hongyu Lin,Xianpei Han,Le Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ScaleBox是一个高保真、可扩展的代码沙箱系统，通过自动化特殊裁判、细粒度并行执行和配置驱动评估，显著提升了大规模代码训练的验证准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码沙箱在高并发下验证不准且效率低，无法满足大规模LLM代码训练的需求。

Method: 自动化特殊裁判生成与管理、细粒度并行执行与多节点协调、配置驱动评估套件。

Result: ScaleBox显著提升代码验证准确性、效率，在RLVR训练中提升LiveCodeBench性能和训练稳定性，优于启发式基线。

Conclusion: ScaleBox提供了可靠、高吞吐量的基础设施，有效促进大规模代码训练的研究与开发。

中文摘要：代码沙箱已成为提升大型语言模型编码能力的关键基础设施，为强化学习训练和评估提供可验证的反馈。然而，现有系统在高并发工作负载下无法提供准确的验证和效率。我们提出了ScaleBox，一个高保真和可扩展的系统，旨在解决大规模代码训练中的这些限制。ScaleBox引入了自动化特殊裁判生成与管理、跨测试用例的细粒度并行执行以及无缝的多节点协调，以及一个配置驱动的评估套件，用于可重复的基准测试。一系列实验表明，ScaleBox显著提高了代码验证的准确性和效率。我们进一步的RLVR实验显示，ScaleBox在LiveCodeBench上的性能和训练稳定性都有显著提升，大幅优于启发式匹配基线。通过提供可靠和高吞吐量的基础设施，ScaleBox促进了大规模代码训练中更有效的研究和开发。

Original abstract: Code sandboxes have emerged as a critical infrastructure for advancing the coding capabilities of large language models, providing verifiable feedback for both RL training and evaluation. However, existing systems fail to provide accurate verification and efficiency under high-concurrency workloads. We present ScaleBox, a high-fidelity and scalable system designed to address these limitations in large-scale code training. ScaleBox introduces automated special-judge generation and management, fine-grained parallel execution across test cases with seamless multi-node coordination, and a configuration-driven evaluation suite for reproducible benchmarking. A series of experiments demonstrates that ScaleBox significantly enhances code verification accuracy and efficiency. Our further RLVR experiments show that ScaleBox substantially improves both performance on LiveCodeBench and training stability, significantly outperforming heuristic-matching baselines. By providing a reliable and high-throughput infrastructure, ScaleBox facilitates more effective research and development in large-scale code training.

</details>


### [5] [A Longitudinal Analysis of Good First Issue Practices and Newcomer Pull Requests in Popular OSS Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27532v2)
*Hirotatsu Hoshikawa,Hidetake Tanaka,Kazumasa Shimari,Raula Gaikovina Kula,Kenichi Matsumoto*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究发现GFI标签比例自2024年起下降，但新手参与度稳定，而合并率从61.9%降至42.2%，表明新手引导面临供应和成功率的双重下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开源项目中“good first issue”引导机制随时间的变化，以帮助维护者和研究人员适应不断演变的开发实践。

Method: 分析37个热门GitHub仓库（30个使用GFI标签）四年间的406,826个问题和1,117个新手GFI拉取请求，使用统计检验和回归分析。

Result: GFI标签比例自2024年1月显著下降，新手参与度稳定在27%，但合并率从61.9%降至42.2%，初始提交特征与合并结果无显著关联。

Conclusion: 新手对GFI的兴趣稳定，但GFI可用性和成功率下降，维护者需同时维持GFI标签和审查支持以缩小差距。

中文摘要：开源软件项目依赖有效的新手引导来维持其社区。开源项目广泛采用“good first issue”（GFI）标签来标识适合初学者的任务。随着开发实践的不断演变，理解这些引导机制随时间的变化对维护者和研究人员都很重要。本研究分析了2021年7月至2025年6月四年间37个热门GitHub仓库（其中30个使用GFI标签）中的406,826个问题和1,117个新手GFI拉取请求。我们发现，虽然带有GFI标签的问题的比例在前三年保持稳定，但从2024年1月开始出现统计上显著的下降，且项目间差异很大，无法通过仓库年龄或编程语言解释。尽管供应侧下降，新手对GFI问题的参与度仍稳定在约27%，表明GFI标签保持一致的吸引力。考察这种参与的结果，我们发现新手GFI拉取请求的合并率从61.9%下降到42.2%。初始拉取请求的特征（如描述长度和代码大小）与合并结果无显著关联，表明成功不能仅由初始提交的数量特征预测。总之，这些发现揭示了新手对GFI的稳定兴趣与基于GFI的引导的可用性和成功率下降之间日益扩大的差距，强调了维护者需要同时维持GFI标签和审查支持。

Original abstract: Open-source software (OSS) projects rely on effective newcomer onboarding to sustain their communities. OSS projects widely adopt "good first issue" (GFI) labels to highlight beginner-friendly tasks. As development practices continue to evolve, understanding how these onboarding mechanisms change over time is important for both maintainers and researchers. This study analyzes 406,826 issues and 1,117 newcomer GFI pull requests across 37 popular GitHub repositories (30 of which use GFI labels) over a four-year period from July 2021 to June 2025. We find that while the proportion of issues with GFI labels remained stable during the first three years, it underwent a statistically significant decline beginning in January 2024, with substantial variation across projects not explained by repository age or programming language. Despite this supply-side decline, newcomer engagement with GFI issues remains stable at approximately 27%, suggesting that GFI labels maintain consistent attractiveness. Examining the outcomes of this engagement, we find that the merge rate of newcomer GFI pull requests declined from 61.9% to 42.2%. Initial pull request characteristics such as description length and code size show no significant association with merge outcomes, indicating that success is not predicted by the quantitative characteristics of the initial submission alone. Together, these findings reveal a widening gap between stable newcomer interest in GFIs and the declining availability and success of GFI-based onboarding, underscoring the need for maintainers to sustain both GFI labeling and review support.

</details>


### [6] [GenAI in Software Engineering: The Role of Technology Acceptance Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27642v1)
*Oscar Johansson,Jürgen Börstler,Nauman bin Ali*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 以UTAUT为例，探讨GenAI在软件工程中接受度的未来研究方向，强调贝叶斯分析的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多组织希望将GenAI融入软件开发，但技术接受模型在SE研究中应用有限，需要明确未来研究重点以促进GenAI接受度。

Method: 回顾UTAUT的基础文献和SE特定文献，分析其在GenAI中的新兴应用。

Result: 确定了三个未来研究重点：细化构念、改进操作化、结合贝叶斯分析。

Conclusion: UTAUT结合贝叶斯分析可用于理解个体层面障碍，但需考虑其他理论。

中文摘要：背景：许多组织热衷于将生成式人工智能（GenAI）融入其软件开发流程。技术接受模型，如技术接受与使用的统一理论（UTAUT），传统上用于识别个体层面接受新技术的障碍，并可促进向GenAI的过渡。然而，UTAUT在软件工程（SE）研究中的应用仍然有限。目标：以UTAUT为例，确定GenAI接受度未来研究的关键领域，包括贝叶斯方法在数据分析中的作用。方法：我们回顾了UTAUT的基础文献和SE特定文献，并分析了其在SE中GenAI的新兴应用。结果：我们确定了未来研究的三个重点：（1）识别并细化构念以考虑GenAI的特性和变革性影响；（2）改进操作化实践以增强构念效度和跨研究可比性；（3）结合贝叶斯分析，通过整合先验知识、迭代模型更新和场景模拟来支持小样本推断。结论：UTAUT是与贝叶斯分析结合以获得关于SE中GenAI使用的个体层面障碍的实践见解的合适候选，但应考虑其他理论。

Original abstract: Context: Many organizations are keen to incorporate generative~AI (GenAI) into their software development processes. Technology acceptance models, such as the Unified Theory of Acceptance and Use of Technology (UTAUT), are traditionally used to identify individual-level barriers to the acceptance of new technologies and can facilitate the transition to GenAI. However, UTAUT has seen limited use within software engineering (SE) research. Objective: Using UTAUT as an example, to identify key areas for future research on GenAI acceptance, including the role of Bayesian approaches for data analysis. Method: We review foundational and SE-specific literature on UTAUT and analyze its emerging applications for GenAI in SE. Results: We identify three priorities for future research: (1) identifying and refining constructs to account for GenAI's nature and transformational impact; (2) improving operationalization practices to strengthen construct validity and cross-study comparability; and (3) incorporating Bayesian analysis to support small-sample inference by integrating prior knowledge, iterative model updating, and simulation of scenarios. Conclusion: UTAUT is a suitable candidate to combine with Bayesian analysis for practical insights on individual-level barriers to GenAI use in SE, but additional theories should be considered.

</details>


### [7] [Tail-aware N-version Machine Learning Models for Reliable API Recommendation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27647v1)
*Aoi Matsuda,Fumio Machida,David Lo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: NvRec通过使用多个版本的ML模型并基于尾部属性过滤不可靠输出来提升API推荐的可靠性，实验表明五版本配置在真实接受率和拒绝率之间取得更好平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码数据集的长尾分布导致ML模型对尾部API推荐不可靠，需要一种方法来抑制不可靠输出以提高推荐可靠性。

Method: 提出N版本API推荐（NvRec），利用多个不同版本的ML模型，通过分析各模型对每个API方法的性能（尤其关注尾部属性），在推理时基于模型配置文件过滤不可靠推荐，并采用多数投票或限制投票策略确定最终输出。

Result: 在五个模型（CodeBERT、CodeT5、MulaRec、UniXcoder、CodeT5+）上，三版本（CodeT5、MulaRec、UniXcoder）配置最高真实接受率83.8%（拒绝率80.7%），五版本配置最高真实接受率83.1%（拒绝率69.0%），五版本平衡更好。

Conclusion: NvRec能有效提升API推荐的可靠性，五版本配置在真实接受率和拒绝率之间提供更优平衡，建议在实际中采用更多版本以降低拒绝率。

中文摘要：基于机器学习（ML）的API推荐帮助开发人员高效地识别合适的API以补充应用程序代码。然而，用于训练ML模型的代码数据集通常呈现长尾分布，导致API推荐不可靠，尤其是对于位于尾部的较少使用的API方法。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了N版本API推荐（NvRec），它利用N个不同版本的ML模型，通过抑制涉及尾部API的不可靠输出来增强API序列推荐的可靠性。NvRec利用一组可用的ML模型，并根据它们的尾部属性对各个API方法的性能进行分析。生成的模型配置文件在推理时用于过滤掉不可靠的API推荐并确定最终输出。我们使用五个API推荐模型（包括CodeBERT、CodeT5、MulaRec、UniXcoder和CodeT5+）实现了NvRec，并在由可编译Java项目构建的公共基准数据集上进行了评估。对于三版本NvRec，当多数投票限于高度可靠的候选时，CodeT5、MulaRec和UniXcoder的组合实现了83.8%的最高真实接受率，拒绝率为80.7%。相比之下，五版本配置通过简单多数投票实现了83.1%的最高真实接受率，同时将拒绝率降低到69.0%。总体而言，五版本配置在真实接受率和拒绝率之间提供了更好的平衡。

Original abstract: Machine learning (ML)-based API recommendation helps developers efficiently identify suitable APIs to complement the application code. However, code datasets used to train ML models often exhibit a long-tail distribution, leading to unreliable API recommendations, especially for infrequently used API methods at the tail of the distribution. To address this issue, we propose N-version API Recommendation (NvRec), which leverages N different versions of ML models to enhance the reliability of API sequence recommendations by suppressing unreliable outputs entailing tail APIs. NvRec leverages a set of available ML models and profiles their performance on individual API methods with their tail properties. The generated model profile is used at inference time to filter out unreliable API recommendations and determine the final output. We implement NvRec using five API recommendation models, including CodeBERT, CodeT5, MulaRec, UniXcoder, and CodeT5+, and evaluate it on a public benchmark dataset constructed from compilable Java projects. For the three-version NvRec, we find that the combination of CodeT5, MulaRec, and UniXcoder achieves the highest true accept rate of 83.8%, with a rejection rate of 80.7%, when majority voting is restricted to highly reliable candidates. In contrast, the five-version configuration achieves its highest true accept rate of 83.1% with simple majority voting, while reducing the rejection rate to 69.0%. Overall, the five-version configuration offers a better balance between true accept rate and rejection rate.

</details>


### [8] [Privacy Engineering: A Systematic Literature Review](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23696v1)
*Nemania Borovits,Damian Andrew Tamburri,Willem-Jan van den Heuvel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 系统综述了90项研究，识别出隐私工程的十三个维度，形成两个核心，并绘制了生命周期分布图和领域加权结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于GDPR等隐私法规对软件工程的深刻影响，需要系统梳理隐私工程的研究现状，揭示其关键维度和结构。

Method: 采用系统综述与主题综合法，对2018至2025年间90项相关研究进行综合与分析。

Result: 识别出十三个维度，分为PETs/PM/VT和GA/TC/OM两个核心，MS为中介；生命周期映射显示不同阶段聚焦不同维度；领域加权不影响结构，但调整了重点。

Conclusion: 提供了隐私工程的实用地图和可复制的研究支架，并指出了IRM、LM和DMPL等未来优先方向。

中文摘要：根据GDPR的隐私义务日益塑造软件工程。我们通过系统综述和主题综合法综合了2018年至2025年的90项研究，以描绘隐私工程。十三个维度形成了两个反复出现的核心：隐私增强技术（PETs）与隐私度量（PM）和验证与测试（VT）以及治理与问责（GA）与透明度和沟通（TC）和组织措施（OM）。建模与规范（MS）在两个核心之间起中介作用。生命周期映射显示了在需求和设计阶段（MS, GA）、在实现和验证阶段（PETs, VT, PM, TC）以及在运维和退役阶段（GA, OM, 数据主体权利管理（DSRM）、事件响应与管理（IRM）、生命周期管理（LM））的集中点。交接环节将模型链接到规则和测试，将机制链接到度量和部署（如安全区和账本）到治理记录。领域会重新加权但不会改变结构：医疗保健加重了GA与VT和PETs，物联网和边缘计算加重了设备及边缘的PETs与VT和PM，网络测量加重了TC与VT，人工智能和机器学习加重了PETs与PM。IRM、LM和数据最小化与目的限制（DMPL）较少作为主要焦点，指明了未来工作的优先方向。结果提供了一个实用的地图和一个可复制评估和更新的支架。

Original abstract: Privacy obligations under GDPR increasingly shape software engineering. We synthesize 90 studies from 2018 to 2025 using a systematic review with thematic synthesis to chart privacy engineering. Thirteen dimensions form two recurrent cores: Privacy Enhancing Technologies (PETs) with Privacy Metrics (PM) and Verification and Testing (VT) and Governance and Accountability (GA) with Transparency and Communication (TC) and Organizational Measures (OM). Modeling and Specification (MS) mediates between the cores. Lifecycle mapping shows concentrations at requirements and design (MS, GA), at implementation and verification (PETs, VT, PM, TC) and at operation and decommissioning (GA, OM, Data Subject Rights Management (DSRM), Incident Response and Management (IRM), Lifelong Management (LM)). Handoffs link models to rules and tests, mechanisms to metrics and deployments such as enclaves and ledgers to governance records. Domains reweight but do not alter structure: healthcare weights GA with VT and PETs, IoT and edge weight PETs with VT and PM at device and edge, web measurement weights TC with VT, AI and ML weight PETs with PM. IRM, LM and Data Minimization and Purpose Limitation (DMPL) are less often primary foci, signaling priorities for future work. The results provide a practical map and a replication-ready scaffold for assessment and updates.

### [9] [PuzzleMark: Implicit Jigsaw Learning for Robust Code Dataset Watermarking in Neural Code Completion Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27677v1)
*Haocheng Huang,Yuchen Chen,Weisong Sun,Peizhuo Lv,Yuan Xiao,Chunrong Fang,Yang Liu,Xiaofang Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PuzzleMark是一种针对代码数据集的鲁棒水印方法，通过基于代码复杂度的载体选择策略和变量名拼接模式替代共现模式，实现了高验证成功率、低假阳性率和强不可感知性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码数据集面临严重的未经授权使用风险，而基于共现模式的传统水印方法鲁棒性不足，易受检测和去除攻击。

Method: 提出PuzzleMark方法，包括基于代码复杂度的载体选择策略、基于变量名拼接的两种水印策略（替代共现模式），并采用Fisher精确检验进行黑盒验证。

Result: 实现100%验证成功率、0%假阳性率，对模型性能影响可忽略；人工评估平均可疑率≤0.24，四种水印检测方法平均召回率≤30.41%。

Conclusion: PuzzleMark是一种实用且鲁棒的代码数据集水印方法，能有效保护知识产权，并为未来研究提供新方向。

中文摘要：构建和整理高质量代码数据集需要大量资源，因此它们具有宝贵的知识产权。不幸的是，这些数据集目前面临着严重的未经授权使用风险。尽管数字水印提供了一种事后版权认证机制，但现有方法主要基于共现模式，这种模式不够鲁棒，容易受到水印检测和去除攻击。在本文中，我们提出了PuzzleMark，一种针对代码数据集的鲁棒水印方法。为了降低水印暴露风险，PuzzleMark引入了一种载体选择策略，利用代码复杂度评估代码片段作为水印载体的适用性，并选择高适用性的代码片段进行水印嵌入。为了增强水印的鲁棒性，PuzzleMark提出了一种新的拼接模式以替代传统的共现模式，并通过变量名拼接实现了两种水印策略。PuzzleMark根据代码的固有特征自适应地嵌入水印，使其在保持设计简洁性的同时更具隐蔽性。在水印验证方面，PuzzleMark采用Fisher精确检验在黑盒设置下验证可疑模型。实验结果表明，PuzzleMark实现了100%的验证成功率和0%的假阳性率，且对模型性能的影响可忽略不计。我们的人工研究和使用四种最先进水印检测方法的评估均显示，PuzzleMark具有强不可感知性，平均可疑率≤0.24，平均召回率≤30.41%。作为一种实用的数字水印方法，PuzzleMark为代码数据集的知识产权提供了强有力的保护，并为未来研究提供了新的见解。

Original abstract: Constructing and curating high-quality code datasets requires significant resources, making them valuable intellectual property. Unfortunately, these datasets currently face severe risks of unauthorized use. Although digital watermarking offers a post hoc mechanism for copyright authentication, existing methods are predominantly based on the co-occurrence pattern, which is not robust and is susceptible to watermark detection and removal attacks. In this paper, we propose PuzzleMark, a robust watermarking method for code datasets. To reduce the risk of watermark exposure, PuzzleMark introduces a carrier selection strategy that leverages code complexity to evaluate the suitability of code snippets as watermark carriers, and selects those with high suitability for watermarking. To enhance the robustness of the watermark, PuzzleMark proposes a novel concatenation pattern to replace the traditional co-occurrence pattern, and implements two watermarking strategies through variable name concatenation. PuzzleMark adaptively embeds watermarks based on the inherent characteristics of the code, making it more stealthy while maintaining design simplicity. For watermark verification, PuzzleMark employs Fisher's exact test to verify suspicious models under a black-box setting. Experimental results demonstrate that PuzzleMark achieves a 100% verification success rate and a 0% false positive rate, with negligible impact on model performance. Both our human study and our evaluation using four state-of-the-art watermark detection methods show that PuzzleMark exhibits strong imperceptibility, with an average suspicious rate $\leq$ 0.24 and an average recall $\leq$ 30.41%, respectively. As a practical digital watermarking method, PuzzleMark provides strong protection for the intellectual property of code datasets and offers new insights for future research.

</details>


### [10] [Understanding Bugs in Template Engine-Based Applications: Symptoms, Root Causes, and Fix Patterns](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27692v1)
*Kai Gao,Yu Sun,Chang-ai Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首个针对模板引擎应用缺陷的全面研究，分析了1004个缺陷，发现异常渲染结果是最常见症状，语法误用等是主要根因，并提出了修复模式与工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模板引擎应用（TE应用）的独特架构导致缺陷诊断困难，而先前研究主要关注安全性，缺乏对TE应用缺陷的系统研究。

Method: 分析跨5种编程语言、15个模板引擎的1004个应用缺陷，识别症状、根因和修复模式，并基于发现开发了Jinja引擎的两个原型工具。

Result: 异常渲染结果是最常见症状（48.61%），识别17个根因，其中语法误用、数据上下文不匹配和不兼容集成是主要类别；67.92%缺陷在模板内修复，超过20%需修改宿主端逻辑。

Conclusion: 为工具设计、实践和研究提供了可操作建议，并通过原型工具验证了发现的实用性。

中文摘要：模板引擎在现代软件生态系统中是不可或缺的组件，能够跨领域（如Web开发、基础设施即代码和数据工程）生成结构化文档和脚本。然而，基于模板引擎的应用程序（即TE应用）独特的架构特征，包括多语言组合、不透明数据流、延迟验证和复杂集成，给诊断和修复TE应用中的缺陷带来了重大挑战。虽然先前的研究主要关注模板引擎的安全性，但TE应用中的缺陷仍未得到充分研究。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了首个针对TE应用缺陷的综合性研究。通过分析跨五种编程语言、15个模板引擎的1,004个应用缺陷，我们识别了TE应用缺陷的症状、根本原因以及修复它们的常见模式。我们的发现表明，异常渲染结果（例如意外或空白输出）是最普遍的症状（48.61%），通常表现为难以诊断的静默失败。我们识别了17个根本原因，其中语法误用、数据上下文不匹配和不兼容集成是主要类别。此外，我们发现虽然67.92%的缺陷在模板内部被修复，但超过20%的缺陷需要修改宿主端逻辑以解决数据上下文问题。基于这些发现，我们为工具设计者、实践者和研究人员得出了可操作的意义。为展示我们发现的实用价值，我们进一步为Jinja引擎开发了两个原型工具，以促进TE应用的开发和调试。

Original abstract: Template engines are indispensable components in modern software ecosystems, enabling the generation of structured documents and scripts across domains such as web development, Infrastructure as Code, and data engineering. However, the unique architectural characteristics of template engine-based applications (i.e., TE applications), including multi-language composition, opaque data flow, deferred validation, and complex integration, pose significant challenges for diagnosing and resolving bugs in TE applications. While prior research has primarily focused on template engine security, bugs in TE applications remain under-investigated. To bridge this gap, we present the first comprehensive study of TE application bugs. By analyzing 1,004 application bugs across 15 template engines in five programming languages, we identify the symptoms and root causes of TE application bugs and common patterns to fix them. Our findings reveal that Abnormal Rendering Result (e.g., unexpected or blank output) is the most prevalent symptom (48.61%), often manifesting as silent failures that are difficult to diagnose. We identify 17 root causes, with Syntax Misuse, Mismatched Data Context, and Incompatible Integration as the dominant categories. Furthermore, we find that while 67.92% of the bugs are fixed within the template, over 20% require modifications in the host-side logic to resolve data context issues. Based on these findings, we derive actionable implications for tool designers, practitioners, and researchers. To demonstrate the practical utility of our findings, we further develop two prototype tools for the Jinja engine to facilitate the development and debugging of TE applications.

### [11] [LLM-as-a-Judge for Human-AI Co-Creation: A Reliability-Aware Evaluation Framework for Coding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27727v1)
*Md Faizul Ibne Amin,Yutaka Watanobe,Daniel M. Muepu,Haruto Suzuki,Kenta Nanaumi,Md Mostafizer Rahman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于量规的LLM-as-a-Judge框架，用于评估竞赛式人类-AI共创编码，通过多指标协议和轨迹分析验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人类-AI共创环境缺乏严格的评估方法，评判需要可靠、跨模型可比且在多轮交互中可解释，因此需要一种新的评估框架。

Method: 构建了基于量规的LLM-as-a-Judge框架，包括模式约束输出、验证修复、按用户和问题分组拆分防泄漏、参与者级NONBLIND上下文；使用多指标协议（ROC-AUC、PR-AUC、MCC、LogLoss、Brier分数、ECE、Cohen's k、Fleiss' k）评估多个LLM评判者；并通过轨迹级信号（Success-at-Turn、时间、修改变动、CodeBLEU等）分析人类-AI共创过程。

Result: 共创成功集中在早期，Success-at-Turn从第一轮0.8533升至第6轮0.8641；修改行为异质，表明进展可通过增量或重构实现。评判最佳保留分数：ROC-AUC 0.5937，PR-AUC 0.6904，MCC 0.5000；评判者间一致性较低（平均配对Cohen's k=0.1592，Fleiss' k=0.0696）。

Conclusion: 提供了一种可审计、可复现的评估方法，将可靠性感知的LLM评判与轨迹分析结合，为未来AI辅助编码和软件工程提供了实用评估模板。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被用作评估开放式输出的评判者以及AI辅助编程中的共创伙伴；然而，在人类-AI共创环境中的严格评估仍然不成熟，因为评判必须可靠、跨模型可比，并且在多轮交互中可解释。为了解决这一差距，本文提出了一种基于量规的LLM-as-a-Judge框架，用于竞赛式的人类-AI共创编码和软件工程（SE）。该框架围绕模式约束的评判输出、验证与修复机制、按用户和问题分组和拆分以防止轨迹泄露，以及参与者级别的NONBLIND上下文构建。通过一个多指标协议评估多个LLM评判者，涵盖区分度（ROC-AUC、PR-AUC）、阈值化决策质量（MCC）、概率可靠性（LogLoss、Brier分数、ECE）以及评判者间一致性（Cohen's和Fleiss' k）。进一步通过轨迹级信号检查人类-AI共创，包括轮次置信度、成功轮次（Success-at-Turn）、成功时间、修改变动和CodeBLEU。发现共创成功集中在早期，第一个观察到的轮次的Success-at-Turn达到0.8533，并在第6轮稳定在0.8641。然而，修改行为仍然存在异质性，表明富有成效的进展可以通过增量改进或更广泛的重构来实现。在评判方面，最佳保留分数达到ROC-AUC为0.5937，PR-AUC为0.6904，MCC测试为0.5000，而评判者间一致性整体适中（平均配对Cohen's k = 0.1592，Fleiss' k = 0.0696）。总的来说，这项工作提供了一种可审计和可复现的评估方法，将可靠性感知的LLM评判与基于轨迹的人类-AI共创分析联系起来，为未来AI辅助编码和SE提供了实用的评估模板。

Original abstract: LLMs are increasingly employed both as judges for evaluating open-ended outputs and as co-creation partners in AI-assisted programming; yet rigorous evaluation in human-AI co-creation settings remains underdeveloped as judgments must be reliable, comparable across models, and interpretable over multi-turn interaction. To address this gap, a rubric-driven LLM-as-a-Judge framework is presented for contest-style human-AI co-creation in coding and software engineering (SE). The framework is built around schema-constrained judge outputs, validation and repair mechanisms, grouped and split by user and problem to prevent trajectory leakage, and participant-level NONBLIND context. Multiple LLM judges are assessed through a multi-metric protocol covering discrimination (ROC-AUC, PR-AUC), thresholded decision quality (MCC), probabilistic reliability (LogLoss, Brier score, ECE), and inter-judge agreement (Cohen's and Fleiss' k). Human-AI co-creation is further examined through trajectory-level signals, including turn-wise confidence, Success-at-Turn, time-to-success, revision churn, and CodeBLEU. Co-creation success is found to concentrate early, with Success-at-Turn rising to 0.8533 at the first observed turn and stabilizing at 0.8641 by turn 6. Revision behavior, however, remains heterogeneous, suggesting that productive progress can emerge through either incremental refinement or broader restructuring. On the judging side, the best held-out scores reach 0.5937 for ROC-AUC, 0.6904 for PR-AUC, and 0.5000 for MCC test, while inter-judge consistency remains modest overall (mean pairwise Cohen's k = 0.1592, Fleiss' k = 0.0696). Taken together, this work offers an auditable and reproducible evaluation methodology that links reliability-aware LLM judging with trajectory-based analysis of human-AI co-creation, providing a practical evaluation template for future AI-assisted coding and SE.

</details>


### [12] [Multifaceted Hero Developers and Bug-Fixing Outcomes Across Severity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27754v1)
*Amit Kumar,Mahen Gandhi,Meher Bhardwaj,Hrishikesh Ethari,Sonali Agarwal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 多面英雄主义在开源项目中普遍存在，但技术英雄和社交英雄重叠很小，表明英雄角色是多维的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作对英雄开发者的定义依赖于单一度量标准，忽略了贡献的多面性，因此需要多面视角。

Method: 使用三种技术度量（提交次数、涉及文件数、代码变动量）和两种社交度量（问题评论数、评论的问题数）对77个Apache项目进行测量研究，分析英雄普遍性、重叠和错误修复结果。

Result: 所有度量下英雄项目常见，但技术英雄和社交英雄重叠仅0.10；71.4%技术英雄有强社交活动，仅24.2%社交英雄有强技术活动；修复率和重新开启率差异不大但排名随严重性变化。

Conclusion: 英雄主义不是单一角色，多面视角更可靠，有助于开发者优先级排序和错误分配。

中文摘要：开源项目通常依赖于一小群高度活跃的贡献者，称为英雄开发者。先前的工作表明，英雄开发者在许多开源软件和企业项目中很常见，但谁有资格成为英雄在很大程度上取决于所选的贡献度量标准。基于代码的度量标准识别出专注于实现的开发者，而基于讨论的度量标准则强调协调和沟通；这些度量标准捕捉了贡献的不同方面。我们使用三种技术度量（提交次数、涉及的不同文件数、代码变动量）和两种社交度量（问题评论数、评论过的不同问题数）对77个Apache软件基金会项目进行了多面英雄主义的度量敏感研究。我们考察了英雄的普遍性、英雄集合之间的重叠，以及通过修复率和重新开启率衡量的严重性级别的错误修复结果。结果表明，在所有度量标准下英雄项目都很常见，但识别的英雄在不同方面存在显著差异。技术英雄集合与社交英雄集合的合并Jaccard重叠仅为0.10。跨方面不对称性很明显：71.4%的技术英雄表现出强烈的社交活动，而只有24.2%的社交英雄表现出强烈的技术活动。修复率和重新开启率的差异不大，但英雄类别排名因严重性级别和结果度量而异。这些发现表明，英雄主义不是一个单一的、与度量标准无关的角色。多面视角能够更可靠地理解关键贡献者，并更好地支持开发者优先级排序和严重性感知的错误分配。

Original abstract: Open-source projects often rely on a small group of highly active contributors known as hero developers. Prior work shows that hero developers are common in many OSS and enterprise projects, yet who qualifies as a hero depends heavily on the chosen contribution metric. Code-based metrics identify implementation-focused developers, whereas discussion-based metrics highlight coordination and communication; these metrics capture distinct facets of contribution. We conducted a measurement-sensitive study of multifaceted heroism across 77 Apache Software Foundation projects using three technical measures (commit count, distinct files touched, churn) and two social measures (issue-comment count, number of distinct issues commented on). We examined hero prevalence, overlap among hero sets, and severity-wise bug-fixing outcomes via fix and reopen rates. Results show that hero projects are common under all measures, but identified heroes differ substantially across facets. The pooled Jaccard overlap between technical and social hero sets is only 0.10. Cross-facet asymmetry is evident: 71.4% of technical heroes exhibit strong social activity, while only 24.2% of social heroes show strong technical activity. Fix-rate and reopen-rate differences are modest, yet hero-category rankings vary across severity levels and outcome measures. These findings indicate that heroism is not a single, metric-independent role. A multifaceted perspective offers a more reliable understanding of key contributors and better supports developer prioritisation and severity-aware bug assignment.

</details>


### [13] [The Grand Software Supply Chain of AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27781v1)
*Carmine Cesarano,Martin Monperrus*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了AI供应链的架构层，识别出可验证性、版本管理、可观测性和可追溯性四个结构性缺口，并通过测量开源项目栈揭示了其巨大规模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统依赖低完整性软件，在数据采集到推理各阶段存在风险，而传统供应链机制无法应对AI供应链特有的结构性问题。

Method: 将AI供应链分解为四个架构层（数据采集、模型训练、模型推理和跨领域基础层），识别四个结构性缺口，并测量一个由48个生产级开源项目组成的参考栈的依赖与代码规模。

Result: 识别出可验证性、版本管理、可观测性和可追溯性四个缺口；测量得到参考栈含4,664个直接依赖、11,508个传递包和约3.92亿行代码。

Conclusion: 当前AI系统在供应链管理上存在根本性不足，需要针对这些结构性缺口开发新的供应链机制。

中文摘要：AI系统依赖于低完整性机制的软件，使得AI系统在从数据采集到最终推理的每个阶段都面临风险。本文将AI供应链作为分析的一级对象，将其分解为四个架构层：数据采集、模型训练、模型推理以及一个跨领域的基础层。在这些层中，我们识别出传统供应链机制未能解决的四个结构性缺口：可验证性、版本管理、可观测性和可追溯性。当前的AI系统在所有这四个方面都存在不足：它们带有未声明的行为耦合，没有解析器强制执行；它们无法回滚到已知的正常工作版本；它们在出现破坏性变更时静默退化，而非浮出表面；它们的来源关系几乎无法近似。为了说明AI软件供应链的规模，我们测量了一个由48个生产级开源项目组成的参考栈，该栈声明了4,664个直接依赖，解析到11,508个传递包，总计约3.92亿行代码。

Original abstract: AI systems rest on software with low integrity mechanisms, leaving AI systems exposed across every stage from data acquisition to final inference. This paper makes the AI supply chain a first-class object of analysis, decomposing it across four architectural layers: data acquisition, model training, model inference, and a cross-cutting substrate. Within these layers, we identify four structural gaps that traditional supply chain mechanisms do not address: verifiability, versioning, observability, and traceability.Current AI systems fall short on all of them: they carry undeclared behavioral couplings that no resolver enforces; they cannot be reverted back to known working assemblies; they degrade silently rather than surfacing breaking changes; and their lineage can hardly be approximated. To illustrate the scale of the software supply chain of AI, we measure a reference stack of 48 production-grade open-source projects, which declares 4,664 direct dependencies, resolves to 11,508 transitive packages, and totals roughly 392M lines of code.

### [14] [Test Before You Deploy: Governing Updates in the LLM Supply Chain](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27789v1)
*Mohd Sameen Chishti,Damilare Peter Oyinloye,Jingyue Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出部署侧治理框架（生产契约、风险类别测试、兼容性门控）来管理LLM静默更新导致的行为漂移，通过探索性验证显示针对性测试能发现整体指标遗漏的回归问题，并指出开放挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM作为软件系统依赖，其提供商侧的静默更新可能引入行为漂移，导致各种回归问题，而现有方法缺乏部署侧兼容性管理机制。

Method: 提出了部署侧治理框架，包含三个组件：生产契约（定义模型允许行为）、基于风险类别的测试套件（按部署风险组织测试）、兼容性门控（阻止不合格更新）。并通过多个LLM版本的探索性验证。

Result: 证据表明在特定风险领域进行针对性测试能揭示整体指标遗漏的性能回归。

Conclusion: 将LLM更新管理视为软件供应链治理问题，并规划了将部署侧兼容性控制付诸实践的研究议程。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正日益成为软件系统中的核心依赖。然而，托管的LLM服务通过提供商侧的持续更新而不断演变，且没有明确的版本变更。这些静默更新可能引入行为漂移，导致功能、格式、安全约束或其他应用特定要求的回归。现有方法主要关注回归测试或版本管理，但没有提供在模型不透明演化过程中用于管理兼容性的部署侧机制。本文提出了一个基于三个组件的部署侧治理框架：明确界定模型允许行为规则（生产契约）、按部署风险类别组织的聚焦测试（基于风险类别的测试套件），以及阻止未达到定义的安全和性能标准的更新的发布检查点（兼容性门控）。通过在多个LLM版本上的探索性验证，我们提供了证据表明在特定风险领域进行有针对性的测试可以揭示整体指标遗漏的性能回归。我们还识别出若干开放研究挑战，包括如何系统性地构建有效的测试套件，如何在非确定性系统中设置可靠的性能阈值，以及如何在提供商透明度有限的情况下检测和解释模型漂移。总体而言，我们将LLM更新管理视为一个软件供应链治理问题，并概述了将部署侧兼容性控制付诸实践的研究议程。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used as core dependencies in software systems. However, the hosted LLM services evolve continuously through provider-side updates without explicit version changes. These silent updates can introduce behavioral drift, causing regressions in functionality, formatting, safety constraints, or other application-specific requirements. Existing approaches focus primarily on regression testing or versioning but do not provide deployer-side mechanisms for governing compatibility during opaque model evolution. This paper proposes a deployment-side governance framework based on three components: clearly defined rules for how the model is allowed to behave (production contracts), focused testing organized by deployment risk categories (risk-category-based testing suite), and release checkpoints that block updates unless they meet defined safety and performance standards (compatibility gates). Through exploratory validation across multiple LLM versions, we provide evidence that targeted testing in specific risk areas can uncover performance regressions that overall metrics miss. We also identify several open research challenges, including how to systematically build effective test suites, how to set reliable performance thresholds in non-deterministic systems, and how to detect and explain model drift when providers offer limited transparency. Overall, we frame LLM update management as a software supply chain governance problem and outline a research agenda for putting deployer-side compatibility controls into practice.

</details>


### [15] [Feature-Centric Methodology for Analyzing Cross-Chain NFT Migration Compatibility](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27805v1)
*Mohd Sameen Chishti,Damilare Peter Oyinloye,Jingyue Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种四层NFT架构和四阶段迁移分析方法，用于预测跨链NFT迁移中的功能兼容性，并通过以太坊到Solana的案例验证了方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨链NFT迁移时，不同区块链平台的架构差异导致功能不兼容，现有协议级机制无法解决深层兼容性问题，因此需要一种方法在迁移前预测功能是否可保留。

Method: 基于标准区块链堆栈推导四层NFT架构（加密、状态管理、交易处理、所有权原语），将NFT视为功能束，提出四阶段迁移分析方法：源功能规范、原语级依赖映射、目标平台分析、兼容性评估，将功能分为原生保留、部分不匹配、完全不匹配三类。

Result: 通过对以太坊到Solana NFT迁移的概念验证分析，识别出若干不兼容问题，证明了方法能够发现阻碍无缝迁移的问题。

Conclusion: 该方法可以有效预测跨链NFT迁移中的功能兼容性，为实际迁移提供决策支持，但需进一步扩展到更多平台和复杂场景。

中文摘要：跨链NFT迁移是指将数字资产及其相关功能和保证在不同区块链平台之间转移的过程。然而，这些平台之间的架构差异带来了关键挑战，常常导致功能无法按预期运行。虽然协议级机制可以协调数据传输，但不足以解决由状态组织、交易执行和所有权表示的根本差异引起的更深层次兼容性问题。因此，关键挑战在于在承担昂贵的迁移尝试之前，预测哪些NFT功能可以保留、哪些需要重新设计、以及哪些根本不相容。为了解决这一挑战，我们首先基于标准区块链堆栈推导出一个定制的四层NFT架构，区分加密、状态管理、交易处理和所有权原语，并具有明确的上层依赖关系。基于此架构，我们将NFT概念化为功能束，并将成功的跨链NFT迁移定义为这些功能的保留。以此模型为基础，我们提出了一种四阶段迁移分析方法论，包括源功能规范、原语级依赖映射、目标平台分析和兼容性评估，该方法将每个功能分类为原生保留、部分不匹配或完全不匹配。我们通过对以太坊到Solana NFT迁移的概念验证分析来评估该方法，识别出了一些阻碍无缝NFT迁移的不兼容问题。

Original abstract: Cross-chain NFT migration refers to the process of transferring digital assets along with their associated functionalities and guarantees between distinct blockchain platforms. However, architectural divergences among these platforms introduce critical challenges, often resulting in features that fail to behave as intended. While protocol-level mechanisms can coordinate data transfer, they are insufficient to resolve deeper compatibility issues arising from fundamental differences in state organization, transaction execution, and ownership representation. Thus, the critical challenge lies in predicting which NFT features can be preserved, which require redesign, and which are fundamentally incompatible, prior to undertaking costly migration attempts. To address this challenge, we first derive a tailored four-layer NFT architecture based on standard blockchain stacks, distinguishing cryptographic, state-management, transaction-processing, and ownership primitives, with explicit upward dependencies. Building on this architecture, we conceptualize an NFT as a bundle of features and define successful cross-chain NFT migration as the preservation of these features. Grounded in this model, we propose a four-phase migration analysis methodology comprising source feature specification, primitive-level dependency mapping, target platform profiling, and compatibility assessment, which classifies each feature as natively preserved, partially mismatched, or completely mismatched. We evaluate this methodology through a proof-of-concept analysis of Ethereum-to-Solana NFT migration, identifying several incompatibility issues that hinder seamless NFT migration.

</details>


### [16] [Requirements Debt in AI-Enabled Perception Systems Development: An Industrial RE4AI Perspective](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27825v1)
*Hina Saeeda,Soniya Abraham*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过专家访谈，首次将技术债务理论与AI需求工程相结合，识别了在AI驱动的汽车感知系统中，演化功能与非功能需求如何导致需求债务的机制，包括语义漂移、验证积压、集成债务、保证滞后、合规偏差等，并指出这些债务会跨数据、模型和系统工件传播，影响系统的可审计性、可靠性和认证准备度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI在汽车感知系统中的集成使得需求从静态变为动态演化，而当前缺乏对这类变更的文档化、验证和追溯，导致技术债务积累。需求债务作为技术债务的关键子类型尚未被充分研究，因此有必要概念化并实证探索其产生和传播机制。

Method: 采用半结构化访谈法，对来自13家国际汽车公司和3家欧洲研究机构的16位专家进行访谈，并使用主题分析法对数据进行定性分析。

Result: 识别了需求债务的两类关键机制：演化功能性需求导致的语义漂移、验证积压和集成债务；演化非功能性需求导致保证滞后、合规偏差以及透明性/可靠性债务。这些机制相互作用，在数据、模型和系统工件中传播债务，损害安全关键感知系统的可审计性、可靠性和认证准备度。

Conclusion: 本研究是首批将技术债务理论与RE4AI结合的实证工作，揭示了AI汽车感知系统中需求债务的根源与传播路径，为后续缓解策略和系统设计提供了理论基础。

中文摘要：人工智能在汽车感知系统中的集成将需求从静态规范转变为由数据、模型和运行环境塑造的持续演化的实体。当此类变更未得到一致记录、验证和追溯时，会累积为需求债务（ReD），这是技术债务中一个未被充分探索但至关重要的子类型。本研究概念化并实证研究了演化的功能性和非功能性需求如何在支持AI的汽车感知系统生命周期中创造和传播需求债务。我们与来自13家国际汽车公司和3家欧洲研究机构的专家进行了16次半结构化访谈，并使用主题分析法分析数据。作为首批将技术债务理论与RE4AI相结合的实证研究之一，本研究识别了关键的需求债务机制。演化的功能性需求（例如，算法更新、传感器融合、架构变更、实时约束）在验证滞后于快速迭代时，驱动语义漂移、验证积压和集成债务。同时，演化的非功能性需求（例如，安全性、网络安全、可靠性、可扩展性、透明性、可信赖性）在标准和伦理期望发生变化时，造成保证滞后、合规偏差以及透明性和可靠性债务。这些相互作用的机制在数据、模型和系统工件中传播需求债务，削弱了安全关键感知系统的可审计性、可靠性和认证准备度。

Original abstract: AI integration in automotive perception systems shifts requirements from static specifications to continuously evolving entities shaped by data, models, and operating contexts. When such changes are not consistently documented, validated, and traced, they accumulate as Requirements Debt (ReD), an underexplored but critical subtype of technical debt. This study conceptualises and empirically investigates how evolving functional and non-functional requirements create and propagate ReD across the AI-enabled automotive perception system lifecycle. We conducted 16 semi-structured interviews with experts from 13 international automotive companies and 3 European research institutes, and analysed the data using thematic analysis. As one of the first empirical studies connecting technical debt theory with RE4AI, the work identifies key ReD mechanisms. Evolving functional requirements (e.g., algorithm updates, sensor fusion, architectural changes, real-time constraints) drive semantic drift, validation backlogs, and integration debt when verification lags behind rapid iteration. In parallel, evolving non-functional requirements (e.g., safety, cybersecurity, reliability, scalability, transparency, trustworthiness) create assurance lag, compliance misalignment, and transparency and reliability debt as standards and ethical expectations shift. These interacting mechanisms propagate ReD across data, models, and system artefacts, undermining auditability, reliability, and certification readiness in safety-critical perception systems.

</details>


### [17] [An Empirical Evaluation of Code Smell Detection in Angular Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27893v1)
*Maykon Nunes,Emanuel Coutinho,Carla Bezerra,Ivan Machado*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过灰色文献综述识别出11种Angular特有代码异味，并开发了自动化静态分析工具，实现高精度检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Angular项目中缺乏对特有代码异味的系统性认知，开发者面临架构管理和代码质量挑战，需要目录和自动检测工具。

Method: 采用灰色文献综述收集社区知识，识别并分类Angular代码异味；基于目录实现静态分析工具；使用人工验证数据集评估检测性能。

Result: 识别11种Angular代码异味，6种与React共享；工具在所有异味上准确率>0.88，F1-score在0.89-1.00之间。

Conclusion: 首个Angular特有代码异味目录证实了自动化检测的可行性与有效性，为前端代码质量提升奠定了基础。

中文摘要：Angular是开发大规模动态Web应用程序最广泛采用的框架之一。随着项目范围和复杂性的增加，开发者在管理架构和维护整洁、模块化代码方面面临日益严峻的挑战。这些挑战通常会导致设计缺陷，即所谓的代码异味。虽然先前的研究已经对React特有的异味进行了分类，但关于Angular特有异味及其表现形式的知识仍然有限。本研究通过灰色文献综述调查了Angular代码异味，整合了社区知识和技术讨论。从收集的来源中，识别出11种不同的Angular代码异味，其中6种也出现在基于React的系统中，表明某些问题是跨框架的。每种异味都进行了分析、举例，并根据其技术特征进行了分组。基于生成的目录，我们实现了一个自动化静态分析工具来检测Angular代码异味。该工具使用人工验证的数据集进行了实证评估，并通过标准信息检索指标评估其有效性。评估结果表明，所有异味均具有高检测性能，准确率超过0.88，F1分数在0.89到1.00之间。研究结果揭示了诸如组件过载、重复逻辑和低效模板绑定等反复出现的问题，强化了系统性检测支持的相关性。本研究提出了首个源自灰色文献的Angular特有代码异味目录，并展示了自动化检测的可行性和有效性，为未来旨在提高前端代码质量的实证研究和工具开发奠定了坚实基础。

Original abstract: Angular is one of the most widely adopted frameworks for developing large-scale, dynamic web applications. As projects increase in scope and complexity, developers face growing challenges in managing architecture and maintaining clean, modular code. These challenges often lead to design flaws, commonly referred to as code smells. While React-specific smells have been cataloged in prior studies, limited knowledge exists regarding Angular-specific smells and how they manifest. This study investigates Angular code smells through a grey literature review, consolidating community knowledge and technical discussions. From the collected sources, 11 distinct Angular code smells were identified, 6 of which also occur in React-based systems, suggesting that some issues are cross-framework. Each smell was analyzed, exemplified, and grouped according to its technical characteristics. Based on the resulting catalog, we implemented an automated static analysis tool to detect Angular code smells. The tool was empirically evaluated using a manually validated dataset, and its effectiveness was assessed through standard information retrieval metrics. The evaluation results indicate high detection performance across all smells, achieving accuracy values above 0.88 and F1-scores ranging from 0.89 to 1.00. The findings reveal recurring issues such as component overloading, duplicated logic, and inefficient template bindings, reinforcing the relevance of systematic detection support. This study presents the first catalog of Angular-specific code smells derived from grey literature and demonstrates the feasibility and effectiveness of automated detection, providing a solid foundation for future empirical studies and tool development aimed at improving front-end code quality.

</details>


### [18] [From Mirage to Grounding: Towards Reliable Multimodal Circuit-to-Verilog Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27969v2)
*Guang Yang,Xing Hu,Xiang Chen,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文发现MLLMs在将电路图翻译为RTL代码时存在“幻象”现象：模型忽略视觉输入，仅凭标识符语义生成代码，并提出了VeriGround模型通过匿名化和偏好对齐来缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前MLLMs在视觉到代码生成任务中存在可靠性问题，尤其是在电路图翻译为RTL代码时，模型可能依赖标识符语义而非视觉信息，导致安全隐患，亟需揭示并解决这类隐蔽缺陷。

Method: 构建C2VEVAL数据集和正常/匿名协议评估8个MLLM以量化幻象效应；提出VeriGround（4B）模型，结合标识符匿名化、拒绝增强和D-ORPO偏好对齐训练，提升视觉基础能力。

Result: VeriGround在正常/匿名模式下分别达到46.11%/42.51%的Functional Pass@1，错误拒绝率仅1.20%/0.00%，对空白图像拒绝率>92%；正常模式下与GPT-5.4性能相当，匿名模式下显著优于所有基线。

Conclusion: VeriGround证明了真正的视觉基础，表明通过标识符匿名化和偏好对齐可有效消除幻象，提升MLLMs在视觉到代码生成中的可信度。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）越来越多地被用于将视觉产物翻译成代码，从UI模型到HTML，从科学图表到Python脚本。电路图可以被视为硬件的视觉领域特定语言：它编码了时序、拓扑和比特级语义，这些对于随意检查是不可见的，但一旦在硅片中制造出来就具有安全性。因此，将这些图翻译成寄存器传输级（RTL）代码代表了视觉到代码生成的极端可靠性测试。我们揭示了一种我们称之为“幻象”（Mirage）的现象：用空白图像替换电路图会使Pass@k保持不变甚至更高，因为模型绕过了视觉输入，而是利用模块头中的标识符语义来检索规范的RTL模板。这构成了一类新的、高度隐蔽的AI辅助代码生成缺陷，直接削弱了MLLMs的可信度。为了量化这种效应，我们构建了C2VEVAL，并在配对的正常/匿名协议下评估了8个MLLM，其中匿名模式将图和模块头中的所有标识符匿名化；所有模型的匿名模式分数急剧下降，证实了高正常模式准确率在很大程度上是一种幻象。然后，我们提出了VeriGround（4B），该模型通过标识符匿名化、拒绝增强和D-ORPO（决策聚焦ORPO）偏好对齐进行训练，该对齐上调了关键的生成或拒绝令牌。VeriGround在正常/匿名模式下分别实现了46.11%/42.51%的功能Pass@1，错误拒绝率仅为1.20%/0.00%，同时保持对空白图像超过92%的拒绝率。仅凭4B参数，VeriGround在正常模式下与GPT-5.4性能相当，在匿名模式下显著优于所有基线，证实了真正的视觉基础。

Original abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly used to translate visual artifacts into code, from UI mockups into HTML to scientific plots into Python scripts. A circuit diagram can be viewed as a visual domain-specific language for hardware: it encodes timing, topology, and bit level semantics that are invisible to casual inspection yet safety critical once fabricated in silicon. Translating such diagrams into register-transfer-level(RTL) code therefore represents an extreme reliability test for vision-to-code generation. We reveal a phenomenon we call Mirage: replacing a circuit diagram with a blank image leaves Pass@k unchanged or even higher, because models bypass the visual input and instead exploit identifier semantics in the module header to retrieve canonical RTL templates. This constitutes a new, highly covert class of defect in AI-assisted code generation that directly undermines MLLMs' trustworthiness. To quantify the effect, we construct C2VEVAL and evaluate eight MLLMs under a paired Normal/Anony protocol in which Anony mode anonymizes all identifiers in both the diagram and the module header; Anony-mode scores drop sharply across all models, confirming that high Normal-mode accuracy is largely a Mirage. We then propose VeriGround (4B), trained with identifier anonymization, refusal augmentation, and D-ORPO (Decision-Focused ORPO) preference alignment that up-weights pivotal generate-or-refuse tokens. VeriGround achieves Functional Pass@1 of 46.11%/42.51%(Normal/Anony) with a False Refusal Rate of only 1.20%/0.00%, while maintaining >92% Refusal Rate on blank images. With only 4B parameters, VeriGround performs on par with GPT-5.4 under Normal and significantly outperforms all baselines under Anony, confirming genuine visual grounding.

</details>


### [19] [Beyond Code, We Are People: A Systematic Mapping of 25 Years of Literature on Soft Skills in Agile Development Teams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28101v1)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用系统文献映射方法，分析2000年1月至2025年5月间来自主要科学数据库的97项研究。

Result: 识别出沟通、适应性、团队合作和领导力等关键软技能，发现其与敏捷角色（如Scrum团队）的关联，明确了Scrum为主要敏捷方法，并指出文献中缺乏角色特定软技能研究等空白。

中文摘要：软件开发是一项社会技术和以人为本的事业，其中人的因素直接影响质量、生产力和创新能力。在此背景下，计算领域的职业发展超越了技术精通，需要专业人员具备应对持续变化和协作需求的能力。其中，非技术技能（软技能）尤为突出，涵盖了社会、情感和沟通维度，对于团队效率和软件项目的成功至关重要。尽管其重要性已得到认可，但在过去25年中（这一时期内行业广泛采纳了敏捷方法）仍缺乏对最相关软技能的系统映射。这一空白限制了软件开发中人文与技术方面的整合。本研究呈现了一项系统文献映射，分析了2000年1月至2025年5月间来自主要科学数据库的97项研究。结果识别出沟通、适应性、团队合作和领导力等反复出现的能力，以及它们与敏捷环境中不同角色的关联。同时确定了所采用的主要敏捷方法（尤其是Scrum），以及文献中的关键空白，例如缺乏针对特定角色的软技能研究。研究结果可为研究人员、教育工作者和实践者在设计课程、培训策略和符合人文因素的组织实践方面提供支持，并强化了在培养协作与创新专业人才过程中整合社会与技术维度的重要性。

Original abstract: Software development is a sociotechnical and human-centered endeavor in which human factors directly influence quality, productivity, and innovation capacity. In this context, career development in computing goes beyond technical mastery, requiring competencies that enable professionals to deal with continuous change and collaborative demands. Among these, non-technical skills (soft skills) stand out, encompassing social, emotional, and communicational dimensions essential to team effectiveness and the success of software projects. Despite their recognized importance, there is still a need for a systematic mapping of the most relevant soft skills over the past 25 years, a period marked by the adoption of agile approaches in industry. This gap limits the integration of human and technical aspects in software development. This study presents a systematic mapping of the literature, analyzing 97 studies published between January 2000 and May 2025 across major scientific databases. The results identify recurring competencies such as communication, adaptability, teamwork, and leadership, as well as their association with different roles in agile contexts. The main agile approaches adopted, particularly Scrum, are also identified, along with key gaps in the literature, such as the lack of studies on role specific soft skills. The findings can support researchers, educators, and practitioners in designing curricula, training strategies, and organizational practices aligned with human factors, reinforcing the importance of integrating social and technical dimensions in the development of collaborative and innovative professionals.

### [20] [Hierarchical Fault Detection and Diagnosis for Transformer Architectures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28118v2)
*Sigma Jahan,Saurabh Singh Rajput,Tushar Sharma,Mohammad Masudur Rahman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出DEFault++，通过层次学习和故障传播图实现Transformer故障的检测、组件定位和原因诊断，并构建DEFault-bench基准，显著提升故障诊断和修复准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer故障难以检测和定位，因为损失和数值正常且症状不指向具体组件，现有技术无法有效追踪根本原因。

Method: 提出DEFault++，采用层次学习框架，首先检测故障，然后通过故障传播图（FPG）识别受影响组件，最后定位组件内原因，并构建含5556个标记运行的DEFault-bench基准用于训练和评估。

Result: DEFault++在故障检测上F1达0.826-0.909，优于四种基线；开发者研究中修复准确率从57.1%提升至83.3%。

Conclusion: Transformer故障诊断需要组件级测量和架构感知推理，而非仅依赖模型级行为；DEFault-bench为后续研究提供了基准。

中文摘要：Transformer现在支撑着工业和研究中关键的AI系统。然而，它们的故障可以在没有运行时错误的情况下悄悄改变模型行为，现有技术几乎无法将这些故障追溯到其组件和根本原因。这类故障之所以逃避检测，是因为损失和数值保持正常，而可见的症状很少能确定是哪个组件负责。我们提出了DEFault++，一种基于层次学习的技术，它首先检测故障，然后识别受影响的组件，最后找出组件内的原因，帮助开发者有效调试Transformer模型。DEFault++利用故障传播图（FPG）组织组件级运行时测量，FPG是架构依赖路径上的结构先验，并报告每个诊断背后的证据。为了训练和评估它，我们构建了DEFault-bench，一个包含5556个标记运行的基准测试，这些运行来自七个模型、九个任务以及编码器和解码器架构的变异测试。DEFault++在故障检测上优于四种先前技术，达到了0.826-0.909的F1分数，在21名参与者的开发者研究中，它将修复准确率从57.1%提高到83.3%。这些结果表明，Transformer故障诊断受益于组件级测量和架构感知推理，而不仅仅是模型级行为，DEFault-bench为Transformer故障诊断的进一步研究提供了基础。

Original abstract: Transformers now underpin critical AI systems across industry and research. Yet their faults can silently alter model behavior without runtime errors, and existing techniques offer little support for tracing these failures to their component and root cause. Such faults evade detection because loss and numerical values stay normal, and the visible symptom rarely identifies the component responsible. We present DEFault++, a hierarchical learning-based technique that first detects a fault, then identifies the affected component, and finally the cause within it, helping developers effectively debug transformer models. DEFault++ organizes component-level runtime measurements with a Fault Propagation Graph (FPG), a structural prior over the architecture's dependency paths, and reports the evidence behind each diagnosis. To train and evaluate it, we construct DEFault-bench, a benchmark of 5,556 labeled runs from mutation testing across seven models, nine tasks, and both encoder and decoder architectures. DEFault++ improves fault detection over four prior techniques, reaching an F1 of 0.826--0.909, and in a developer study with 21 participants, it raises repair accuracy from 57.1% to 83.3%. These results show that transformer fault diagnosis benefits from component-level measurements and architecture-aware reasoning rather than model-level behavior alone, and DEFault-bench provides a foundation for further research on transformer fault diagnosis.

</details>


### [21] [To Vibe Research or Not to Vibe Research? Generative AI in Qualitative Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00922v1)
*Katja Karhu,Kari Smolander,Jussi Kasurinen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过总结和分析定性研究中生成式AI的现有讨论，从研究哲学（小q和大Q）及其他影响因素（技能、伦理、偏好）进行梳理。

Result: 研究哲学（小q或大Q）是决定生成式AI是否适用的主要标准，同时技能、伦理和个人偏好也影响研究者决策。

Conclusion: 生成式AI在定性研究中的使用需结合研究哲学、技能、伦理和个人偏好综合考量，软件工程研究者应谨慎对待。

Original abstract: There has been intense debate among qualitative researchers about whether generative AI is suitable for qualitative research. In this paper, we summarize the broader ongoing discussion of generative AI in qualitative research and its implications for software engineering researchers. The qualitative research approach, small-q (positivist or post-positivist) or Big Q (non-positivist), is among the major criteria for determining whether generative AI can be used in qualitative research. In addition to research philosophy and research approach, skills, ethics, and personal preferences also play a role in researchers' decisions about whether to use AI in qualitative research.

### [22] [Claw-Eval-Live: A Live Agent Benchmark for Evolving Real-World Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28139v2)
*Chenxin Li,Zhengyang Tang,Mingxin Huang,Yunlong Lin,Shijue Huang,Shengyuan Liu,Bowen Ye,Rang Li,Lei Li,Benyou Wang,Yixuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Claw-Eval-Live 是一个实时工作流代理基准测试，通过可刷新的信号层和固定快照评估模型，发现当前模型通过率最高仅66.7%，工作流自动化远未解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理基准测试冻结任务集且仅评分最终响应，难以评估代理对动态工作流需求的适应性和任务执行的可验证性。

Method: 构建Claw-Eval-Live基准，分离可刷新的信号层与时间戳快照，从公共需求信号生成任务，并使用确定性检查与结构化LLM判断进行评分。

Result: 领先模型通过率仅66.7%，无模型达70%；HR、管理和多系统业务工作流是瓶颈；模型通过率相似但完成度可能不同；任务区分集中在中段。

Conclusion: 工作流代理评估应双重基于新鲜外部需求和可验证代理行动，当前自动化水平远未成熟。

中文摘要：LLM 代理被期望完成跨软件工具、商业服务和本地工作空间的端到端工作单元。然而，许多代理基准测试在发布时冻结了策划的任务集，并且主要对最终响应进行评分，这使得难以根据不断变化的工作流需求评估代理，或验证任务是否被执行。我们引入了 Claw-Eval-Live，一个用于工作流代理的实时基准测试，它将一个可刷新的信号层（跨版本从公共工作流需求信号更新）与一个可重现、带时间戳的发布快照分开。每个发布版本都是从公共工作流需求信号构建的，当前版本使用 ClawHub Top-500 技能，并物化为具有固定夹具、服务、工作空间和评分器的受控任务。对于评分，Claw-Eval-Live 记录执行轨迹、审计日志、服务状态和运行后工作空间工件，当证据足够时使用确定性检查，仅对语义维度使用结构化 LLM 判断。该发布版本包含 105 个任务，涵盖受控商业服务和本地工作空间修复，并在共享公共通过规则下评估了 13 个前沿模型。实验表明，可靠的工作流自动化远未解决：领先模型仅通过 66.7% 的任务，且没有模型达到 70%。失败按任务族和执行面结构化，HR、管理和多系统业务工作流是持续瓶颈，而本地工作空间修复相对容易但尚未饱和。仅靠排行榜排名是不够的，因为具有相似通过率的模型可能在整体完成度上存在差异，并且任务级区分集中在一个中等难度的任务区间。Claw-Eval-Live 建议，工作流代理评估应双重基于新鲜的外部需求和可验证的代理行动。

Original abstract: LLM agents are expected to complete end-to-end units of work across software tools, business services, and local workspaces. Yet many agent benchmarks freeze a curated task set at release time and grade mainly the final response, making it difficult to evaluate agents against evolving workflow demand or verify whether a task was executed. We introduce Claw-Eval-Live, a live benchmark for workflow agents that separates a refreshable signal layer, updated across releases from public workflow-demand signals, from a reproducible, time-stamped release snapshot. Each release is constructed from public workflow-demand signals, with ClawHub Top-500 skills used in the current release, and materialized as controlled tasks with fixed fixtures, services, workspaces, and graders. For grading, Claw-Eval-Live records execution traces, audit logs, service state, and post-run workspace artifacts, using deterministic checks when evidence is sufficient and structured LLM judging only for semantic dimensions. The release contains 105 tasks spanning controlled business services and local workspace repair, and evaluates 13 frontier models under a shared public pass rule. Experiments reveal that reliable workflow automation remains far from solved: the leading model passes only 66.7% of tasks and no model reaches 70%. Failures are structured by task family and execution surface, with HR, management, and multi-system business workflows as persistent bottlenecks and local workspace repair comparatively easier but unsaturated. Leaderboard rank alone is insufficient because models with similar pass rates can diverge in overall completion, and task-level discrimination concentrates in a middle band of tasks. Claw-Eval-Live suggests that workflow-agent evaluation should be grounded twice, in fresh external demand and in verifiable agent action.

</details>


### [23] [Unsafe and Unused? A History of Utility Code in Mature Open Source Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28146v1)
*Brandon Keller,Kaitlin Yandik,Angela Ngo,Andy Meneely*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过对七个开源项目的纵向分析，发现util文件比非util文件更可能涉及漏洞（2.75倍），且其使用模式揭示了开发者意图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 帮助开发者避免创建不安全且未使用的util文件，因为util文件常被滥用，可能导致重复代码、增加维护成本和安全风险。

Method: 对七个长期开源项目的Git仓库进行纵向挖掘，每30天分析一次快照，共1773个快照覆盖147个项目年，追踪util文件的重命名和生命周期。

Result: util文件涉及漏洞的可能性是非util文件的2.75倍；util文件在项目中具有普遍性和长期性。

Conclusion: util文件的命名约定虽旨在促进代码重用，但可能带来更高的安全风险，开发者应谨慎使用并加强代码审查。

中文摘要：文件名是向其他开发者传达源代码信息的一种简洁方式。其中一种约定是util。通常理解为“utility”的缩写，文件名中包含util通常表明该文件包含可能广泛有用或可重用的代码。一些项目大量使用此约定，例如，Apache Tomcat服务器在路径名中包含925个util文件，占树中所有源代码文件的17.9%。虽然命名的意图可能是防止重复代码和减少工作量，但util代码随着时间的推移实际会发生什么？项目在成熟过程中是否会远离util代码？util文件是否被同事使用，还是由其作者维护和使用？我们的工作目标是帮助开发者在开发项目时避免创建不安全且未使用的util文件。我们对七个具有较长开发历史的开源项目（Linux内核、Django、FFmpeg、httpd、Struts、systemd、Tomcat）的Git仓库进行了纵向挖掘研究。我们分析了这些项目中util的使用、复杂性、开发者协作和安全性之间潜在的关联。我们的纵向分析以30天为间隔测量每个项目的整个历史，总共覆盖147个项目年开发中的1773个快照。我们在每个30天快照进行重命名追踪，以检查util文件在其整个生命周期中的情况。例如，我们发现util文件涉及漏洞的可能性是非util文件的2.75倍。虽然每个项目可以采用自己的命名约定，但util文件的普遍性和长期性显示了更广泛的开发者意图，有助于理解软件开发的社交技术本质。

Original abstract: Filenames are a concise means of conveying information about source code to fellow developers. One such convention is util. Commonly understood to stand for "utility", filenames with the letters util are often an indication that the file contains code that may be broadly useful or reusable. Some projects use this convention heavily, for example, the Apache Tomcat server contains 925 files with util in the path name, which is 17.9% of all source code files in the tree. While the intent of the name may be to prevent duplicate code and reduce workload, what actually happens to util code over time? Do projects move away from util code as they mature? Are util files being used by fellow colleagues, or maintained and used by their author? The goal of our work is to help developers avoid creating unsafe and unused util files when developing their projects. We conducted a longitudinal mining study of the Git repositories of seven open source projects that have a long development history (Linux kernel, Django, FFmpeg, httpd, Struts, systemd, Tomcat). We analyzed how util usage, complexity, developer collaboration, and security are potentially correlated within these projects. Our longitudinal analysis was measured at 30-day intervals throughout the entire history of each project, resulting in 1773 snapshots over 147 project-years of development. We conducted rename tracking at every 30-day snapshot to examine util files over their entire lifetime in a codebase. For example, we found that a util file can be as much as 2.75 times more likely to be involved in a vulnerability than non-util files. While every project can adopt their own naming conventions, the ubiquity and longevity of util files shows a broader developer intent that is useful for understanding the socio-technical nature of software development.

</details>


### [24] [DEPTEX: Organization-First, Open Source Dependency Risk Monitoring](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00179v1)
*Henry Ruckman-Utting,Vrushal Nedungadi,Taiga Okuma,LeTian Wang,Stephen Ehebald,Mohammad A. Tayebi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Deptex是一个基于图、以组织为先的供应链风险管理平台，通过执行路径主导性和大语言模型语义验证，结合可编程的“即代码”治理引擎，实现上下文感知的主动风险缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源软件依赖管理工具存在严重的警报疲劳问题，因为它们将风险视为组件固有属性而忽略语义上下文，并强制企业采用僵化的合规框架，难以应对大规模系统性风险。

Method: Deptex采用组织优先的图方法，提出执行路径主导性（EPD）技术，融合代码属性图（CPG）切片与大语言模型（LLM）语义验证来计算漏洞的真实操作爆炸半径，并将治理抽象为可编程的“即代码”引擎。

Result: Deptex能够计算漏洞的真实操作爆炸半径，并通过动态策略、自定义资产层级和API集成实现上下文感知的治理，从被动扫描转向主动风险管理。

Conclusion: 通过上下文感知的治理，Deptex实现了主动、高效且一致的供应链风险管理，克服了现有工具的警报疲劳和僵化合规问题。

中文摘要：开源软件（OSS）依赖引入了难以规模化管理的系统性风险。现有的软件成分分析（SCA）和可达性工具将风险视为组件的固有属性，忽略了语义上下文，并迫使企业陷入僵化的合规框架，从而产生严重的警报疲劳。我们提出Deptex，一个以组织为先、基于图的平台，将供应链风险视为涌现性质。Deptex引入了执行路径主导性（EPD），融合代码属性图（CPG）切片与大语言模型（LLM）语义验证，以计算漏洞的真实操作爆炸半径。为处理定制化合规，Deptex将治理抽象为可编程的“即代码”引擎，使安全团队能够原生地执行动态拉取请求策略、自定义资产层级和外部API集成。通过从被动扫描转向上下文感知的治理，Deptex实现了主动、高效且一致的供应链风险管理。

Original abstract: Open-source software (OSS) dependencies introduce systemic risks that are difficult to manage at scale. Existing Software Composition Analysis (SCA) and reachability tools generate severe alert fatigue by treating risk as an intrinsic component property, ignoring semantic context and forcing enterprises into rigid compliance frameworks. We present Deptex, an organization-first, graph-based platform treating supply chain risk as emergent. Deptex introduces Execution Path Dominance (EPD), fusing Code Property Graph (CPG) slicing with Large Language Model (LLM) semantic verification to calculate a vulnerability's true operational blast radius. To handle bespoke compliance, Deptex abstracts governance into a programmable ``As Code'' engine, enabling security teams to natively enforce dynamic pull request policies, custom asset tiers, and external API integrations. By shifting from reactive scanning to context-aware governance, Deptex enables proactive, efficient, and aligned supply chain risk management.

</details>


### [25] [What Characterizes a Software Leader? Identifying Leadership Practices from Practitioners Social Media](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00191v1)
*Murilo Coelho,Denivan Campos,Mariana Maia Bezerra,Matheus Paixao,Allysson Allex Araujo,Savio Freire*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过对116篇从业者文章的内容分析，识别出103种软件项目领导者实践，分为五大类，发现软件领导力主要关联管理和人际实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对日常实践中领导力的体验和展现缺乏洞察。

Method: 对Dev.to社区的116篇从业者文章进行内容分析，包括系统收集、筛选、编码和相关分析。

Result: 识别出103种实践，分为五类，包括推荐和不推荐的实践；最常推荐的是人际技能、团队管理和管理技能；最常不推荐的是微观管理、适得其反的工作模式和沟通风格。

Conclusion: 软件领导力主要与管理和人际实践相关，而非技术；概念图可作为理解软件开发环境中领导力的参考。

中文摘要：上下文：领导力已在管理和敏捷软件开发领域得到广泛研究；然而，先前的研究主要关注正式角色和预定义的领导模型，对软件从业者在日常实践中如何体验和展现领导力的洞察有限。目标：我们的目标是识别和分类软件从业者根据其专业经验所感知和报告的领导力实践。方法：我们对在Dev.to在线社区发表的116篇从业者撰写的文章进行了内容分析。文章被系统收集、筛选和编码，从而提取、进行相关分析和分类基于从业者叙述的领导力实践。结果：我们识别出103种软件项目领导者的实践，区分了推荐的和不推荐的。这些实践被组织成五个类别：人员管理与开发、流程与执行、专业与个人成长、沟通与表述以及战略愿景。最常被推荐的实践包括培养与实践人际技能、管理与委派团队工作以及练习与发展管理技能，而微观管理、适得其反的工作模式和适得其反的沟通风格则是最常被不推荐的实践。我们将所有实践组织成一个概念图。结论：研究结果表明，软件领导力主要与管理和人际实践相关，而非技术专长。得出的概念图总结了这些实践，可作为理解软件开发环境中领导力的参考。

Original abstract: Context: Leadership has been extensively studied in management and agile software development; however, prior research predominantly focuses on formal roles and predefined leadership models, offering limited insight into how leadership is experienced and demonstrated by software practitioners in everyday practice. Objective: Our goal is to identify and categorize leadership practices as perceived and reported by software development practitioners based on their professional experiences. Method: We conducted a content analysis of 116 practitioner-authored articles published on the Dev.to online community. Articles were systematically collected, screened, and coded, resulting in the extraction, correlation analysis and categorization of leadership practices grounded in practitioners narratives. Results: We identified 103 practices for software project leaders, distinguished between recommended and discouraged ones. These practices were organized into five categories: People Management & Development, Processes & Execution, Professional & Personal Growth, Communication & Articulation and Strategic Vision. The most recurrent recommended practices include Cultivating & Practicing Interpersonal Skills, Managing & Delegating Team Work, and Practicing & Developing Managerial Skills, whereas Micromanagement, Counterproductive Work Patterns, and Counterproductive Communication Styles emerged as the most frequent discouraged practices. We organized all practices into a conceptual map. Conclusion: The findings indicate that software leadership is mainly associated with managerial and interpersonal practices rather than technical expertise. The resulting conceptual map summarizes these practices and can serve as a reference for understanding leadership in software development contexts.

</details>

### [26] [The Inverse-Wisdom Law: Architectural Tribalism and the Consensus Paradox in Agentic Swarms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27274v1)
*Dahlia Shehata,Ming Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究多agent swarm中的共识悖论与架构部落主义，提出通用agent理论与评估，可迁移至coding agent设计。

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模实验证明多智能体系统中存在“共识悖论”，即智能体更倾向于内部一致而非真理，并提出异质性命令作为安全架构准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战多智能体系统研究中“群体智慧”的默认假设，揭示其可能优先内部一致而非外部真理的潜在风险。

Method: 在GAIA、Multi-Challenge和SWE-bench三个基准上进行36个实验，涵盖12,804条轨迹，评估Gemini 3.1 Pro、Claude Sonnet 4.6和GPT-5.4三个模型的交互行为。

Result: 发现逆智慧定律、逻辑饱和现象和架构部落不对称，并确定部落系数和谄媚权重为群体失败的主要机制。

Conclusion: 提出异质性命令作为构建弹性多智能体架构的基本安全要求，强调合成器接收逻辑的关键作用。

中文摘要：随着人工智能向多智能体系统（MAS）发展以解决复杂工作流，研究范式基于一个公理性假设，即智能体协作反映了“群体智慧”。我们通过形式化共识悖论来挑战这一假设：一种现象，即智能体群体优先考虑内部架构一致性而非外部逻辑真理。通过包含12,804条轨迹的36个实验，跨越三个最先进的基准（GAIA、Multi-Challenge和SWE-bench），我们证明了逆智慧定律：在亲缘主导的群体中，增加逻辑智能体会增加错误轨迹的稳定性，而非真理的概率。引入额外的逻辑审计会使系统收敛到逻辑饱和状态，其中内部熵为零而事实错误为单位。通过评估三个最先进的模型（Gemini 3.1 Pro、Claude Sonnet 4.6和GPT-5.4）之间的交互，我们建立了架构部落不对称作为Transformer权重的机械定律。我们证明了终端群体完整性严格受限于合成器的接收逻辑，而非聚合智能体质量。我们将部落系数和谄媚权重定义为群体失败的主要机械决定因素。最后，我们将异质性命令确立为弹性智能体架构的基本安全要求。

Original abstract: As AI transitions toward multi-agent systems (MAS) to solve complex workflows, research paradigms operate on the axiomatic assumption that agent collaboration mirrors the "Wisdom of the Crowd". We challenge this assumption by formalizing the Consensus Paradox: a phenomenon where agentic swarms prioritize internal architectural agreement over external logical truth. Through a 36 experiments encompassing 12,804 trajectories across three state-of-the-art (SOTA) benchmarks (GAIA, Multi-Challenge, and SWE-bench), we prove the Inverse-Wisdom Law: in kinship-dominant swarms, adding logical agents increases the stability of erroneous trajectories rather than the probability of truth. The introduction of additional logical audits converges the system toward a Logic Saturation where internal entropy hits zero while factual error hits unity. By evaluating the interaction between the 3 preeminent SOTA models (Gemini 3.1 Pro, Claude Sonnet 4.6, and GPT-5.4), we establish the Architectural Tribalism Asymmetry as a mechanistic law of transformer weights. We demonstrate that terminal swarm integrity is strictly gated by the synthesizer's receptive logic, rather than aggregate agent quality. We define the Tribalism Coefficient and the Sycophantic Weight as the primary mechanistic determinants of swarm failure. Finally, we establish the Heterogeneity Mandate as a foundational safety requirement for resilient agentic architectures.

</details>


### [27] [Machine Collective Intelligence for Explainable Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27297v1)
*Gyoung S. Na,Chanyoung Park*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出机器集体智能，多agent协同符号发现，可迁移至多agent代码优化协作。

TL;DR: 本文提出机器集体智能，整合符号主义和元启发式，自动发现控制方程，相比深度神经网络外推误差降低六个数量级，参数压缩至5-40个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从经验观测推导可解释且可外推的控制方程是科学长期挑战，现有AI虽擅长函数逼近但无法发现此类方程，成为AI驱动科学发现的瓶颈。

Method: 提出机器集体智能范式，集成符号主义和元启发式，通过多推理智能体协同生成、评估、批评和整合符号假设，实现控制方程的自主进化发现。

Result: 在确定性、随机性及未表征动力学系统中自动恢复控制方程；外推误差相比深度神经网络降低六个数量级；模型参数从0.5-100万压缩至5-40个可解释参数。

Conclusion: 该研究标志着AI向自主发现原则性科学方程的重要转变，推动了可解释AI在科学发现中的应用。

中文摘要：从经验观测中推导控制方程是科学中长期存在的挑战。尽管人工智能（AI）在函数逼近方面展现了强大的能力，但发现可解释且可外推的方程仍然是现代AI的基本局限，构成了AI驱动科学发现的核心瓶颈。本文提出机器集体智能，一种统一范式，整合了计算智能中两个基本但不同的传统——符号主义和元启发式——以实现控制方程的自主和进化发现。它协调多个推理智能体，通过协同生成、评估、批评和整合来进化其符号假设，实现超越单智能体推理的科学发现。在由确定性、随机性或先前未表征动力学支配的科学系统中，机器集体智能自主恢复了底层控制方程，无需依赖手工构建的领域知识。此外，与深度神经网络相比，所得方程将外推误差降低了多达六个数量级，同时将0.5-100万个模型参数压缩为仅5-40个可解释参数。这项研究标志着人工智能向自主发现原则性科学方程的重要转变。

Original abstract: Deriving governing equations from empirical observations is a longstanding challenge in science. Although artificial intelligence (AI) has demonstrated substantial capabilities in function approximation, the discovery of explainable and extrapolatable equations remains a fundamental limitation of modern AI, posing a central bottleneck for AI-driven scientific discovery. Here, we present machine collective intelligence, a unified paradigm that integrates two fundamental yet distinct traditions in computational intelligence--symbolism and metaheuristics--to enable autonomous and evolutionary discovery of governing equations. It orchestrates multiple reasoning agents to evolve their symbolic hypotheses through coordinated generation, evaluation, critique, and consolidation, enabling scientific discovery beyond single-agent inference. Across scientific systems governed by deterministic, stochastic, or previously uncharacterized dynamics, machine collective intelligence autonomously recovered the underlying governing equations without relying on hand-crafted domain knowledge. Furthermore, the resulting equations reduced extrapolation error by up to six orders of magnitude relative to deep neural networks, while condensing 0.5-1 million model parameters into just 5-40 interpretable parameters. This study marks an important shift in AI toward the autonomous discovery of principled scientific equations.

</details>


### [28] [METASYMBO: Multi-Agent Language-Guided Metamaterial Discovery via Symbolic Latent Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27300v1)
*Jianpeng Chen,Wangzhi Zhan,Dongqi Fu,Junkai Zhang,Zian Jia,Ling Li,Wei Wang,Dawei Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent框架用于材料发现，虽领域不同，但其多agent语言引导和符号演化方法对agent设计有借鉴。

TL;DR: MetaSymbO是一个多智能体框架，利用符号驱动潜在演化实现语言引导的超材料发现，显著提升了结构有效性和语言引导分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有逆设计方法需要明确数值目标，不适合早期探索；LLM能理解自然语言但缺乏几何和物理知识，导致无法直接用于超材料设计。

Method: 提出MetaSymbO框架，包含三个智能体（设计者、生成器、监督者），并引入符号驱动潜在演化，通过可编程算子对解耦的潜在因素进行组合、修改和优化。

Result: 结构有效性提升（对称性34%，周期性98%），语言引导分数提高6-7%，同时保持结构新颖性；定性分析证实符号逻辑算子的有效性；实际案例验证实用能力。

Conclusion: MetaSymbO有效实现了语言引导的超材料发现，克服了现有方法在早期探索阶段的局限，并展现了实际应用潜力。

中文摘要：超材料发现旨在寻找其几何结构能够诱导目标力学行为的微结构材料。现有的逆设计方法可以高效生成候选方案，但它们通常需要明确的数值属性目标，不太适合早期探索阶段，而研究人员在此阶段通常从用自然语言表达的不完整约束和定性意图开始。大型语言模型可以解释这类意图，但缺乏几何感知和物理属性有效性。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了MetaSymbO，一个通过符号驱动潜在演化进行语言引导的超材料发现的多智能体框架。具体来说，MetaSymbO包含三个智能体：一个设计者，用于解释自由形式的设计意图并检索语义一致的基础结构；一个生成器，用于在解耦的潜在空间中合成候选微结构；以及一个监督者，用于提供快速的属性感知反馈以进行迭代优化。为了超越从文献和训练数据中复现已知样本的限制，我们进一步引入了符号驱动的潜在演化，它在推理时对解耦的潜在因素应用可编程算子，以组合、修改和优化结构。大量实验表明：(i) 与最先进的基线相比，MetaSymbO在对称性方面将结构有效性提高了34%，在周期性方面提高了近98%；(ii) 与先进的推理LLM相比，MetaSymbO在保持优异结构新颖性的同时，语言引导得分提高了约6-7%；(iii) 定性分析证实了符号逻辑算子在实现可编程语义对齐方面的有效性；(iv) 关于拉胀、高刚度超材料设计的实际案例研究进一步验证了其实用能力。

Original abstract: Metamaterial discovery seeks microstructured materials whose geometry induces targeted mechanical behavior. Existing inverse-design methods can efficiently generate candidates, but they typically require explicit numerical property targets and are less suitable for early-stage exploration, where researchers often begin with incomplete constraints and qualitative intents expressed in natural language. Large language models can interpret such intents, but they lack geometric awareness and physical property validity. To address this gap, we propose MetaSymbO, a multi-agent framework for language-guided Metamaterial discovery via Symbolic-driven latent evOlution. Specifically, MetaSymbO contains three agents: a Designer that interprets free-form design intents and retrieves a semantically consistent scaffold, a Generator that synthesizes candidate microstructures in a disentangled latent space, and a Supervisor that provides fast property-aware feedback for iterative refinement. To move beyond the limitations of reproducing known samples from literature and training data, we further introduce symbolic-driven latent evolution, which applies programmable operators over disentangled latent factors to compose, modify, and refine structures at inference time. Extensive experiments demonstrate that (i) MetaSymbO improves structural validity by up to 34% in symmetry and nearly 98% in periodicity compared to state-of-the-art baselines; (ii) MetaSymbO achieves about 6-7% higher language-guidance scores while maintaining superior structure novelty compared to advanced reasoning LLMs; (iii) qualitative analyses confirm the effectiveness of symbolic logic operators in enabling programmable semantic alignment; and (iv) realworld case studies on auxetic, high-stiffness metamaterial design further validate its practical capability.

### [30] [Heterogeneous Scientific Foundation Model Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27351v1)

Method: 提出Eywa框架，为领域基础模型添加语言模型推理接口，支持单代理（EywaAgent）、多代理（EywaMAS）和规划编排（EywaOrchestra）三种模式。

Result: 在物理、生命和社会科学领域的实验中，Eywa在结构化/领域特定数据任务上性能提升，并减少了对语言推理的依赖。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的智能代理系统已展现出强大的能力。然而，它们依赖语言作为通用接口，这从根本上限制了它们在许多现实问题中的适用性，尤其是在科学领域，其中已经开发出领域特定的基础模型来处理超出自然语言的专门任务。在这项工作中，我们引入了Eywa，一个异构代理框架，旨在将语言中心的系统扩展到更广泛的科学基础模型类别。Eywa的关键思想是使用基于语言模型的推理接口增强领域特定的基础模型，使语言模型能够指导对非语言数据模态的推理。这种设计使得通常针对专门数据和任务优化的预测性基础模型能够参与到代理系统中的更高层次推理和决策过程中。Eywa可以作为单代理流程的即插即用替代方案（EywaAgent），或通过用专业代理替换传统代理集成到现有的多代理系统中（EywaMAS）。我们进一步研究了一种基于规划的编排框架，其中规划器动态协调传统代理和Eywa代理，以解决跨异构数据模态的复杂任务（EywaOrchestra）。我们在涵盖物理、生命和社会科学的多个科学领域评估了Eywa。实验结果表明，Eywa在涉及结构化和领域特定数据的任务上提高了性能，同时通过与专业基础模型的有效协作减少了对基于语言推理的依赖。

Original abstract: Agentic large language model systems have demonstrated strong capabilities. However, their reliance on language as the universal interface fundamentally limits their applicability to many real-world problems, especially in scientific domains where domain-specific foundation models have been developed to address specialized tasks beyond natural language. In this work, we introduce Eywa, a heterogeneous agentic framework designed to extend language-centric systems to a broader class of scientific foundation models. The key idea of Eywa is to augment domain-specific foundation models with a language-model-based reasoning interface, enabling language models to guide inference over non-linguistic data modalities. This design allows predictive foundation models, which are typically optimized for specialized data and tasks, to participate in higher-level reasoning and decision-making processes within agentic systems. Eywa can serve as a drop-in replacement for a single-agent pipeline (EywaAgent) or be integrated into existing multi-agent systems by replacing traditional agents with specialized agents (EywaMAS). We further investigate a planning-based orchestration framework in which a planner dynamically coordinates traditional agents and Eywa agents to solve complex tasks across heterogeneous data modalities (EywaOrchestra). We evaluate Eywa across a diverse set of scientific domains spanning physical, life, and social sciences. Experimental results demonstrate that Eywa improves performance on tasks involving structured and domain-specific data, while reducing reliance on language-based reasoning through effective collaboration with specialized foundation models.
