### [31] [Safe Bilevel Delegation (SBD): A Formal Framework for Runtime Delegation Safety in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27358v1)
*Yuan Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent安全委托框架，对agent安全设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出安全双层委派（SBD）框架，通过双层优化动态调整委派的安全-效率权衡，并给出三个理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏运行时动态调整委派安全-效率权衡的机制，无法适应执行中任务上下文变化。

Method: 将委派形式化为双层优化：外层学习上下文相关权重，内层在安全约束下优化策略，通过连续委派度控制自主程度。

Result: 证明了安全性单调性、内层收敛性和可问责性传播界三个理论结果，并在三个高风险领域指定了评估协议。

Conclusion: SBD提供了形式化的运行时委派安全框架，理论上有保障，实证验证后续进行。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）代理被部署在高风险环境中，如何安全地将子任务委派给专门的子代理这一问题变得至关重要。现有工作在设计时解决多代理架构选择问题，或提供广泛的实证指南，但两者都没有提供一种运行时机制，能够根据执行过程中任务上下文的变化动态调整安全性-效率权衡。我们提出了安全双层委派（SBD），一种用于层次化多代理系统中运行时委派安全的形式化框架。SBD将任务委派形式化为一个双层优化问题：外层元权重网络φ学习上下文相关的安全性-效率权重λ(s) ∈ [0,1]；内层在概率安全约束P(安全) ≥ 1-δ下优化委派策略π。连续委派度α ∈ [0,1]控制转移到每个子代理的决策权限大小，在完全人工覆盖（α=0）和完全自主执行（α=1）之间平滑插值。我们建立了三个理论结果：(1) 安全性单调性——较高的外层安全权重产生弱安全的内层策略；(2) 内层策略收敛性——在标准光滑性假设下，内层问题的投影梯度下降线性收敛；(3) 可问责性传播界——将责任分配到多跳委派链上，并具有可证明的单代理上限。我们在三个高风险领域——医学AI（MIMIC-III）、金融风险控制（标普500）和教育代理监督（ASSISTments）——实例化了SBD，指定了数据集、安全约束集、基线和评估协议。本手稿完整呈现了形式化框架和理论结果；按照此处所述协议进行的实证验证已计划，并将在后续修订中报告。

Original abstract: As large language model (LLM) agents are deployed in high-stakes environments, the question of how safely to delegate subtasks to specialized sub-agents becomes critical. Existing work addresses multi-agent architecture selection at design time or provides broad empirical guidelines, but neither provides a runtime mechanism that dynamically adjusts the safety-efficiency trade-off as task context changes during execution.
  We propose Safe Bilevel Delegation (SBD), a formal framework for runtime delegation safety in hierarchical multi-agent systems. SBD formulates task delegation as a bilevel optimization problem: an outer meta-weight network phi learns context-dependent safety-efficiency weights lambda(s) in [0,1]; an inner loop optimizes the delegation policy pi subject to a probabilistic safety constraint P(safe) >= 1-delta. The continuous delegation degree alpha in [0, 1] controls how much decision authority is transferred to each sub-agent, interpolating smoothly between full human override (alpha=0) and fully autonomous execution (alpha=1).
  We establish three theoretical results: (1) Safety Monotonicity--higher outer safety weight produces a weakly safer inner policy; (2) Inner Policy Convergence--projected gradient descent on the inner problem converges linearly under standard smoothness assumptions; (3) an Accountability Propagation bound that distributes responsibility across multi-hop delegation chains with a provable per-agent ceiling. We instantiate SBD in three high-stakes domains--medical AI (MIMIC-III), financial risk control (S and P 500), and educational agent supervision (ASSISTments)--specifying datasets, safety constraint sets, baselines, and evaluation protocols. This manuscript presents the formal framework and theoretical results in full; empirical validation following the protocols described herein is planned and will be reported in a forthcoming revision.

</details>


### [32] [TADI: Tool-Augmented Drilling Intelligence via Agentic LLM Orchestration over Heterogeneous Wellsite Data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00060v1)
*Rong Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 钻井领域agent系统，LLM编排多工具，可迁移至coding agent。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用DuckDB和ChromaDB双存储架构，设计12个领域专用工具，由LLM通过迭代函数调用编排，实现多步证据收集和交叉引用，形式化为顺序工具选择问题，并提出EGS评估指标。

Result: 系统无错误解析1,759个DDR XML文件，兼容三种井命名约定，具有95个自动化测试和130题压力测试，案例和消融分析显示工具设计比模型规模更关键。

Conclusion: 在技术操作分析中，领域专用工具设计是提升分析质量的主要因素，而非单纯依赖模型规模。

中文摘要：我们提出了TADI（工具增强钻井智能），一个将钻井操作数据转化为基于证据的分析智能的智能体AI系统。应用于Equinor Volve油田数据集，TADI将1,759份每日钻井报告、选定的WITSML实时对象、15,634条生产记录、地层顶部和射孔数据整合到一个双存储架构中：DuckDB用于对12个表（65,447行）进行结构化查询，ChromaDB用于对36,709个嵌入文档进行语义搜索。十二个领域专用工具由大型语言模型通过迭代函数调用编排，支持多步证据收集，将结构化钻井测量与每日报告叙述进行交叉引用。该系统无错误地解析了所有1,759个DDR XML文件，处理了三种不兼容的井命名约定，并得到95个自动化测试以及涵盖六个操作类别的130个压力问题分类法的支持。我们将智能体的行为形式化为一个顺序工具选择问题，并提出了证据基础分数（EGS）作为一个简单的基础合规代理，基于测量值、归属的DDR引用和所需的答案部分。完整的6,084行、无框架实现是可复现的，只需公开的Volve下载和API密钥，案例研究和定性消融分析表明，领域专用工具设计，而非仅仅是模型规模，是技术操作中分析质量的主要驱动因素。

Original abstract: We present TADI (Tool-Augmented Drilling Intelligence), an agentic AI system that transforms drilling operational data into evidence-based analytical intelligence. Applied to the Equinor Volve Field dataset, TADI integrates 1,759 daily drilling reports, selected WITSML real-time objects, 15,634 production records, formation tops, and perforations into a dual-store architecture: DuckDB for structured queries over 12 tables with 65,447 rows, and ChromaDB for semantic search over 36,709 embedded documents. Twelve domain-specialized tools, orchestrated by a large language model via iterative function calling, support multi-step evidence gathering that cross-references structured drilling measurements with daily report narratives. The system parses all 1,759 DDR XML files with zero errors, handles three incompatible well naming conventions, and is backed by 95 automated tests plus a 130-question stress-question taxonomy spanning six operational categories. We formalize the agent's behavior as a sequential tool-selection problem and propose the Evidence Grounding Score (EGS) as a simple grounding-compliance proxy based on measurements, attributed DDR quotations, and required answer sections. The complete 6,084-line, framework-free implementation is reproducible given the public Volve download and an API key, and the case studies and qualitative ablation analysis suggest that domain-specialized tool design, rather than model scale alone, is the primary driver of analytical quality in technical operations.

### [33] [InteractWeb-Bench: Can Multimodal Agent Escape Blind Execution in Interactive Website Generation?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27419v1)
*Qiyao Wang,Haoran Hu,Longze Chen,Hongbo Wang,Hamid Alinejad-Rokny,Yuan Lin,Min Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多模态agent交互网站生成benchmark，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: InteractWeb-Bench是一个多模态交互基准，通过模拟非专家用户的模糊指令，揭示了前沿MLLM智能体在网站生成中存在的盲执行问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准依赖理想化输入和静态设置，无法反映实际开发中非专家用户模糊、低质量指令导致的语义错位和盲执行问题，亟需一个能模拟真实用户行为的基准。

Method: 引入四种用户智能体和基于需求工程缺陷分类法的指令扰动（模糊、冗余、矛盾），构建包含Clarify、Implement、Verify、Submit统一动作空间的交互式执行环境，支持迭代意图精炼和视觉反馈验证。

Result: 实验表明前沿MLLM智能体在非专家低代码条件下仍陷入盲执行，意图识别和自适应交互能力显著不足。

Conclusion: 需要改进智能体的意图理解与交互能力，以应对实际开发中的指令不完美性。

中文摘要：随着多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）和编码智能体的进步，网站开发已从手动编程转向基于智能体的项目级代码合成。现有基准依赖于理想化的假设，特别是针对结构良好、信息丰富的输入和静态执行环境。相比之下，实际开发受到一个关键瓶颈的制约：非专家用户的模糊、低质量指令与模型理解之间的语义错位，导致了一种我们称之为盲执行（blind execution）的失败模式。为了解决这一差距，我们引入了InteractWeb-Bench，这是首个在非专家低代码用户条件下进行网站生成的多模态交互式基准。InteractWeb-Bench引入了四种类型的用户智能体和基于人物角色的指令扰动，基于需求工程缺陷分类法，系统性地模拟多样化的用户行为，包括模糊性、冗余和矛盾。我们开发了一个用于智能体的交互式执行环境，具有统一的行动空间，包括澄清（Clarify）、实现（Implement）、验证（Verify）和提交（Submit），支持迭代意图精炼、代码合成和基于视觉反馈的验证。大量的实验和分析表明，前沿的基于MLLM的智能体仍然陷入盲执行，暴露了在意图识别和自适应交互方面的局限性。

Original abstract: With the advancement of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) and coding agents, the website development has shifted from manual programming to agent-based project-level code synthesis. Existing benchmarks rely on idealized assumptions, especially for well-structured, information-rich inputs and static execution settings. In contrast, real-world development is constrained by a critical bottleneck: the semantic misalignment between ambiguous, low-quality instructions from non-expert users and model understanding, which results in a failure mode that we term blind execution. To address this gap, we introduce InteractWeb-Bench, the first multimodal interactive benchmark for website generation under non-expert low-code user conditions. InteractWeb-Bench introduces four types of user agents and persona-driven instruction perturbations to systematically simulate diverse user behaviors, including ambiguity, redundancy, and contradiction, grounded in requirement engineering defect taxonomies. We develop an interactive execution environment for agents, featuring a unified action space comprising Clarify, Implement, Verify, and Submit, enabling iterative intent refinement, code synthesis, and visual feedback-based validation. Extensive experiments and analysis reveal that frontier MLLM-based agents remain trapped in blind execution, exposing limitations in intent recognition and adaptive interaction.

### [34] [PRTS: A Primitive Reasoning and Tasking System via Contrastive Representations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27472v1)

Method: PRTS采用目标条件强化学习框架，通过对比学习让状态-动作嵌入与目标嵌入的内积近似目标占用概率，从离线轨迹中提取密集可达性监督，并通过角色感知因果掩码将其融入VLM骨干。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通过强大的视觉-语言先验知识推动了机器人控制的发展。然而，现有的VLA模型主要将预训练视为监督行为克隆，忽视了机器人学习作为需要理解时间任务进展的目标到达过程的本质。我们提出了PRTS（原始推理与任务系统），这是一个通过目标条件强化学习重新定义预训练的VLA基础模型。通过将语言指令视为目标并采用对比强化学习，PRTS学习了一个统一的嵌入空间，其中状态-动作嵌入与目标嵌入的内积近似于对数折扣目标占用概率，即从当前状态-动作到达语言指定目标的概率，从而在静态语义匹配之外定量评估物理可行性。PRTS直接从离线轨迹中提取这种密集的目标可达性监督，无需奖励标注，并通过角色感知因果掩码将其整合到VLM骨干网络中，相比普通行为克隆仅增加极小的开销。这种范式赋予了高层推理系统内在的目标可达性意识，桥接了语义推理和时间任务进展，并进一步有益于目标条件动作预测。PRTS在包含167B token的多样化操作和具身推理数据上预训练，在LIBERO、LIBERO-Pro、LIBERO-Plus、SimplerEnv以及一个包含14个复杂任务的真实世界套件上达到了最先进的性能，特别是在长时域、密集接触和零样本新指令设置中取得了显著提升，证实了注入目标可达性意识能够显著提升通用机器人基础策略的执行成功率和长时域规划能力。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models advance robotic control via strong visual-linguistic priors. However, existing VLAs predominantly frame pretraining as supervised behavior cloning, overlooking the fundamental nature of robot learning as a goal-reaching process that requires understanding temporal task progress. We present \textbf{PRTS} (\textbf{P}rimitive \textbf{R}easoning and \textbf{T}asking \textbf{S}ystem), a VLA foundation model that reformulates pretraining through Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning. By treating language instructions as goals and employing contrastive reinforcement learning, PRTS learns a unified embedding space where the inner product of state-action and goal embeddings approximates the log-discounted goal occupancy, the probability of reaching the language-specified goal from the current state-action, quantitatively assessing physical feasibility beyond static semantic matching. PRTS draws this dense goal-reachability supervision directly from offline trajectories without reward annotations, and folds it into the VLM backbone via a role-aware causal mask, incurring negligible overhead over vanilla behavior cloning. This paradigm endows the high-level reasoning system with intrinsic goal reachability awareness, bridging semantic reasoning and temporal task progress, and further benefits goal-conditioned action prediction. Pretrained on 167B tokens of diverse manipulation and embodied-reasoning data, PRTS reaches state-of-the-art performance on LIBERO, LIBERO-Pro, LIBERO-Plus, SimplerEnv, and a real-world suite of 14 complex tasks, with particularly substantial gains on long-horizon, contact-rich, and zero-shot novel-instruction settings, confirming that injecting goal-reachability awareness significantly improves both execution success and long-horizon planning of general-purpose robotic foundation policies.

### [35] [Belief-Guided Inference Control for Large Language Model Services via Verifiable Observations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27536v1)
*Wenhao Yuan,Chenchen Lin,Jian Chen,Jinfeng Xu,Shuo Yang,Edith Cheuk Han Ngai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于POMDP的推理控制框架，涉及预算感知决策和信念状态，可迁移至agent的推理资源分配。

TL;DR: Veroic是一种用于黑盒LLM服务的自适应推理控制框架，通过部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程建模，利用轻量级可验证观测通道实现预算感知的响应决策，改善质量-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑盒LLM服务中响应可靠性部分可观测且计算成本高，需要自适应分配资源以平衡质量和成本。

Method: 将请求时控制建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），通过聚合异构质量信号构建信念状态，并由预算感知策略决定是否触发更高成本推理。

Result: 在多样化任务上实现了更好的质量-成本权衡、更强的风险估计与校准，以及更鲁棒的长期推理控制。

Conclusion: Veroic框架有效提升了黑盒LLM推理控制的性能和鲁棒性。

中文摘要：在黑盒大语言模型（LLM）服务中，响应可靠性在决策时通常仅部分可观测，而更强的推理路径会带来大量的计算成本，从而引发一个带预算的序贯决策问题：对每个请求，系统应决定默认的低成本响应是否足够可靠，或者是否需要分配额外的计算资源来提高响应质量。在本文中，我们提出Verifiable Observations for Risk-aware Inference Control (Veroic)，一个用于黑盒LLM设置中自适应推理控制的框架，它将请求时控制建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程以捕获部分可观测性和序贯预算关联。它通过将异构质量信号聚合成对潜在响应可靠性的信念状态，从输入-输出对构建轻量级可验证观测通道，然后由预算感知策略使用该状态来决定是返回默认输出还是触发更高成本的推理路径。在多样化任务上的实验表明，Veroic实现了更好的质量-成本权衡、更强的风险估计与校准，以及比竞争基线更鲁棒的长期推理控制。

Original abstract: In black-box large language model (LLM) services, response reliability is often only partially observable at decision time, while stronger inference pathways incur substantial computational cost, inducing a budgeted sequential decision problem: for each request, the system should decide whether the default low-cost response is sufficiently reliable or whether additional computation should be allocated to improve response quality. In this paper, we propose \textbf{Ver}ifiable \textbf{O}bservations for Risk-aware \textbf{I}nference \textbf{C}ontrol (\textsc{Veroic}), a framework for adaptive inference control in black-box LLM settings, which formulates request-time control as a \textit{partially observable Markov decision process} to capture partial observability and sequential budget coupling. It constructs a lightweight verifiable observation channel from the input-output pair by aggregating heterogeneous quality signals into a belief state over latent response reliability, which is then used by a budget-aware policy to decide whether to return the default output or trigger a higher-cost inference pathway. Experiments on diverse tasks show that \textsc{Veroic} achieves improved quality-cost trade-offs, stronger risk estimation and calibration, and more robust long-horizon inference control than competitive baselines.

### [36] [In-Context Examples Suppress Scientific Knowledge Recall in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27540v1)
*Chaemin Jang,Woojin Park,Hyeok Yun,Dongman Lee,Jihee Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 发现in-context example会抑制LLM的知识回忆，对agent使用few-shot策略有警示意义。

TL;DR: LLM在科学推理中，添加上下文示例会抑制其使用预训练知识，导致转向模式拟合，而非知识驱动推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在科学推理任务中，上下文示例是否真的强化了知识运用，还是会产生意外效果。

Method: 在五个科学领域的60个潜在结构恢复任务中，通过添加或不添加上下文示例，观察模型推理策略的变化，涉及6000次试验和四个模型。

Result: 上下文示例导致模型从知识驱动推理转向经验模式拟合，这种位移普遍存在，但准确性影响不一。

Conclusion: 上下文示例可能取代而非强化知识，部署LLM在科学任务时需谨慎。

中文摘要：科学推理很少停留在直接可观察的事物上；它通常需要从数据中揭示隐藏的结构。从化学中估算反应常数到经济中推断需求弹性，这种潜在结构恢复是科学推理与曲线拟合的区别所在。大型语言模型（LLM）通常能够回忆并应用相关的科学公式，但我们表明这种能力出奇地容易被抑制。我们证明，添加上下文中的示例会使模型更少依赖预训练领域知识，即使这些示例是由完全相同的公式生成的。示例非但没有强化基于知识的推导，反而将计算转向了经验模式拟合。我们在五个科学领域的60个潜在结构恢复任务、6000次试验和四个模型中记录了这一知识位移。这种位移在各个领域是一致的，但其准确性后果取决于被置换的策略与替代它的策略的比较：相同的位移可能降低准确性、保持不变，甚至看起来有所提升。然而在所有情况下，模型都偏离了基于知识的推理。对于在科学任务中部署LLM的从业者来说，信息是警示性的：上下文中的示例可能会取代而不是强化它们旨在支持的知识。

Original abstract: Scientific reasoning rarely stops at what is directly observable; it often requires uncovering hidden structure from data. From estimating reaction constants in chemistry to inferring demand elasticities in economics, this latent structure recovery is what distinguishes scientific reasoning from curve fitting. Large language models (LLMs) can often recall and apply relevant scientific formulas, but we show that this ability is surprisingly easy to suppress. We show that adding in-context examples makes models rely less on pretrained domain knowledge, even when those examples are generated by the very same formula. Rather than reinforcing knowledge-driven derivation, examples shift computation toward empirical pattern fitting. We document this knowledge displacement on 60 latent structure recovery tasks across five scientific domains, 6,000 trials, and four models. This displacement is consistent across domains, but its accuracy consequences depend on how the displaced strategy compares to the one that replaces it: the same shift can lower accuracy, leave it unchanged, or appear to improve it. In all cases, however, the model shifts away from knowledge-driven reasoning. For practitioners deploying LLMs on scientific tasks, the message is cautionary: in-context examples may displace, rather than reinforce, the knowledge they are intended to support.

Original abstract: Automatically generating interactive 3D indoor scenes from natural language is crucial for virtual reality, gaming, and embodied AI. However, existing LLM-based approaches often suffer from spatial errors and collisions, in part because common scene representations-raw coordinates or verbose code-are difficult for models to reason about 3D spatial relationships and physical constraints. We propose SpatialGrammar, a domain-specific language that represents gravity-aligned indoor layouts as BEV grid placements with deterministic compilation to valid 3D geometry, enabling verifiable constraint checking. Building on this representation, we develop (1) SG-Agent, a closed-loop system that uses compiler feedback to iteratively refine scenes and enforce collision constraints, and (2) SG-Mini, a 104M-parameter model trained entirely on compiler-validated synthetic data. Across 159 test scenes spanning five scenarios of different complexity, SG-Agent improves spatial fidelity and physical plausibility over prior methods, while SG-Mini performs competitively against larger LLM-based baselines on single-shot generation scenarios.

### [38] [Trace-Level Analysis of Information Contamination in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27586v1)
*Anna Mazhar,Huzaifa Suri,Sainyam Galhotra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统信息污染分析，提供trace测量框架和污染分类，对agent可靠性和验证有直接价值。

TL;DR: 该研究通过在结构化代理工作流中注入扰动来量化不确定性污染，发现了工作流分歧与正确性之间的解耦现象，并提出了污染表现的类型学、检测框架及对验证设计的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构化工作流中的不确定性不仅是输入质量问题，还会影响执行轨迹和最终结果，但现有研究缺乏对其系统性的定量分析和分类。

Method: 将不确定性作为控制变量，向制品衍生表示中注入结构化扰动，在固定工作流下进行日志记录，通过轨迹分歧（计划、工具调用、中间状态）量化污染，并在32个GAIA任务上使用三种语言模型进行614次配对实验。

Result: 发现工作流分歧与答案正确性存在解耦：显著分歧可恢复正确答案，而结构相似却可能输出错误。识别出三种污染表现类型（无声语义损坏、行为绕行恢复、结构性破坏）及其控制流特征，并观察到常用验证护栏失效。

Conclusion: 提出了污染表现的形式化分类、基于轨迹的检测框架，并提供了对目标验证、防御设计和成本控制有影响的实证证据。

中文摘要：在结构化代理工作流中，对异构制品（如PDF、电子表格、幻灯片等）进行推理的情况日益增多，这些工作流迭代地提取、转换和引用外部信息。在这些工作流中，不确定性不仅仅是输入质量问题：它可以重定向分解和路由决策，重塑中间状态，并产生性质不同的执行轨迹。我们通过将不确定性作为控制变量来研究这一现象：我们向制品衍生表示中注入结构化扰动，在全面日志记录下执行固定工作流，并通过计划、工具调用和中间状态中的轨迹分歧来量化污染。在32个GAIA任务的614次配对运行中，使用三种不同的语言模型，我们发现一种解耦现象：工作流可能显著发散却恢复正确答案，或者结构相似却产生错误输出。我们描述了三种表现类型：无声语义损坏、带有恢复的行为绕行、以及结构性破坏及其控制流特征（重路由、扩展执行、提前终止）。我们测量了操作成本，并描述了为何常用的验证护栏无法拦截污染。我们贡献了：（i）结构化工作流中污染表现的形式化分类，（ii）用于检测和定位代理交互中污染的基于轨迹的测量框架，以及（iii）对目标验证、防御设计和成本控制具有影响的实证证据。

Original abstract: Reasoning over heterogeneous artifacts (PDFs, spreadsheets, slide decks, etc.) increasingly occurs within structured agent workflows that iteratively extract, transform, and reference external information. In these workflows, uncertainty is not merely an input-quality issue: it can redirect decomposition and routing decisions, reshape intermediate state, and produce qualitatively different execution trajectories. We study this phenomenon by treating uncertainty as a controlled variable: we inject structured perturbations into artifact-derived representations, execute fixed workflows under comprehensive logging, and quantify contamination via trace divergence in plans, tool invocations, and intermediate state. Across 614 paired runs on 32 GAIA tasks with three different language models, we find a decoupling: workflows may diverge substantially yet recover correct answers, or remain structurally similar while producing incorrect outputs. We characterize three manifestation types: silent semantic corruption, behavioral detours with recovery, and combined structural disruption and their control-flow signatures (rerouting, extended execution, early termination). We measure operational costs and characterize why commonly used verification guardrails fail to intercept contamination. We contribute (i) a formal taxonomy of contamination manifestations in structured workflows, (ii) a trace-based measurement framework for detecting and localizing contamination across agent interactions, and (iii) empirical evidence with implications for targeted verification, defensive design, and cost control.

### [39] [WaferSAGE: Large Language Model-Powered Wafer Defect Analysis via Synthetic Data Generation and Rubric-Guided Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27629v4)
*Ke Xu,Zhongyuan Lian*

Motivation: 半导体制造中晶圆缺陷数据稀缺，且大型专有模型部署成本高、存在隐私问题，需要小型、可本地部署的高效模型。

Method: 三阶段合成管道：聚类清洗去噪、VLM生成缺陷描述并转为结构化评分标准、基于评分标准合成VQA对；双重评估框架（规则+LLM-Judge）；基于课程学习的强化学习（GSPO）与评分标准对齐奖励。

Result: 4B参数Qwen3-VL模型在LLM-Judge上达到6.493，接近Gemini-3-Flash的7.149，且支持完全本地部署。

Conclusion: 小型模型通过领域特定训练可在专业视觉任务上超越大型模型，为隐私保护和经济高效的半导体制造部署提供可行方案。

中文摘要：我们提出了WaferSAGE，一个用于晶圆缺陷视觉问答的小型视觉-语言模型框架。为了解决半导体制造中的数据稀缺问题，我们提出了一个三阶段合成流程，结合结构化评分标准生成以实现精确评估。从有限的标记晶圆图开始，我们采用基于聚类的清洗来过滤标签噪声，然后使用视觉-语言模型生成全面的缺陷描述，并将其转化为结构化评估评分标准。这些评分标准指导VQA对的合成，确保覆盖缺陷类型识别、空间分布、形态和根因分析。我们的双重评估框架通过贝叶斯优化将基于规则的指标与LLM-Judge评分对齐，实现可靠的自动评估。通过基于课程学习的强化学习结合组序列策略优化（GSPO）和与评分标准对齐的奖励，我们的4B参数Qwen3-VL模型获得了6.493的LLM-Judge评分，接近Gemini-3-Flash（7.149），同时支持完全本地部署。我们证明了具有特定领域训练的小型模型可以在专业工业视觉理解上超越专有大型模型，为半导体制造中的隐私保护、低成本部署提供可行路径。

Original abstract: We present WaferSAGE, a framework for wafer defect visual question answering using small vision-language models. To address data scarcity in semiconductor manufacturing, we propose a three-stage synthesis pipeline incorporating structured rubric generation for precise evaluation. Starting from limited labeled wafer maps, we employ clustering-based cleaning to filter label noise, then generate comprehensive defect descriptions using vision-language models, which are converted into structured evaluation rubrics criteria. These rubrics guide the synthesis of VQA pairs, ensuring coverage across defect type identification, spatial distribution, morphology, and root cause analysis.
  Our dual assessment framework aligns rule-based metrics with LLM-Judge scores via Bayesian optimization, enabling reliable automated evaluation. Through curriculum-based reinforcement learning with Group Sequence Policy Optimization (GSPO) and rubric-aligned rewards, our 4B-parameter Qwen3-VL model achieves a 6.493 LLM-Judge score, closely approaching Gemini-3-Flash (7.149) while enabling complete on-premise deployment. We demonstrate that small models with domain-specific training can surpass proprietary large models in specialized industrial visual understanding, offering a viable path for privacy-preserving, cost-effective deployment in semiconductor manufacturing.

</details>


### [40] [Optimization before Evaluation: Evaluation with Unoptimised Prompts Can be Misleading](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27637v1)
*Nicholas Sadjoli,Tim Siefken,Atin Ghosh,Yifan Mai,Daniel Dahlmeier*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 揭示提示优化对模型评估排名的影响，对agent评估流程设计有重要启发。

TL;DR: 提示优化显著影响LLM评估排名，评估时应为每个模型进行提示优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM评估使用统一静态提示模板，而行业实践则针对每个模型优化提示，因此需要研究提示优化对评估结果的影响。

Method: 在公共学术和内部行业基准上，比较使用和不使用提示优化时模型的排名变化。

Result: 提示优化极大地改变了模型排名，表明其对评估结果的显著影响。

Conclusion: 为公平选择最佳模型，评估时应为每个模型进行提示优化。

中文摘要：当前的大型语言模型（LLM）评估框架对所有被评估模型使用相同的静态提示模板。这与常见的行业实践不同，即使用提示优化（PO）技术为每个模型优化提示以最大化应用性能。在本文中，我们研究了提示优化对LLM评估的影响。我们在公共学术和内部行业基准上的结果表明，提示优化极大地影响了模型的最终排名。这凸显了从业者在进行评估以选择给定任务的最佳模型时，需要为每个模型执行提示优化的重要性。

Original abstract: Current Large Language Model (LLM) evaluation frameworks utilize the same static prompt template across all models under evaluation. This differs from the common industry practice of using prompt optimization (PO) techniques to optimize the prompt for each model to maximize application performance. In this paper, we investigate the effect of PO towards LLM evaluations. Our results on public academic and internal industry benchmarks show that PO greatly affects the final ranking of models. This highlights the importance of practitioners performing PO per model when conducting evaluations to choose the best model for a given task.

### [41] [From Context to Skills: Can Language Models Learn from Context Skillfully?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27660v3)
*Shuzheng Si,Haozhe Zhao,Yu Lei,Qingyi Wang,Dingwei Chen,Zhitong Wang,Zhenhailong Wang,Kangyang Luo,Zheng Wang,Gang Chen,Fanchao Qi,Minjia Zhang,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Ctx2Skill多agent自进化框架，从上下文发现技能，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出Ctx2Skill框架，通过多智能体自对弈和跨时间回放实现无监督上下文技能发现与优化，提升语言模型上下文学习能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖昂贵的人工标注或外部反馈，难以从长且技术密集的上下文中自动构建技能。

Method: 采用多智能体自对弈循环，包括挑战者、推理者和裁判，并通过提议者和生成器从失败案例中合成技能更新；引入跨时间回放机制防止对抗性崩溃，选择最佳平衡的技能集。

Result: 在CL-bench的四个任务上，Ctx2Skill在多个骨干模型上一致提升了解答率。

Conclusion: Ctx2Skill能自主生成可迁移的技能，有效增强语言模型在复杂上下文中的推理能力，无需人工干预。

中文摘要：许多现实世界任务要求语言模型（LMs）对超出其参数化知识的复杂上下文进行推理。这需要上下文学习（context learning），即LM直接从给定上下文中学习相关知识。一个直观的解决方案是推理时技能增强：从上下文中提取规则和程序到自然语言技能中。然而，为上下文学习场景构建此类技能面临两个挑战：对于长且技术密集的上下文，手动技能标注成本高昂，以及缺乏用于自动技能构建的外部反馈。在本文中，我们提出Ctx2Skill，一个自演化框架，可以在没有人工监督或外部反馈的情况下自主发现、细化和选择上下文特定技能。其核心是一个多智能体自我对弈循环，包含一个挑战者（生成试探任务和评分标准）、一个推理者（尝试在演化技能集指导下解决它们）和一个中立裁判（提供二元反馈）。关键的是，挑战者和推理者都通过积累的技能演化：专门的提议者和生成器智能体分析失败案例并将其合成为针对双方的目标技能更新，从而实现自动技能发现和细化。为了防止由越来越极端的任务生成和过度专门化的技能积累导致的对抗性崩溃，我们进一步引入了跨时间回放机制，该机制识别出推理者侧在代表性案例上实现最佳平衡的技能集，确保鲁棒和可泛化的技能演化。得到的技能可以插入任何语言模型，以获得更好的上下文学习能力。在来自CL-bench的四个上下文学习任务上评估，Ctx2Skill在多个骨干模型上一致地提高了解决率。

Original abstract: Many real-world tasks require language models (LMs) to reason over complex contexts that exceed their parametric knowledge. This calls for context learning, where LMs directly learn relevant knowledge from the given context. An intuitive solution is inference-time skill augmentation: extracting the rules and procedures from context into natural-language skills. However, constructing such skills for context learning scenarios faces two challenges: the prohibitive cost of manual skill annotation for long, technically dense contexts, and the lack of external feedback for automated skill construction. In this paper, we propose Ctx2Skill, a self-evolving framework that autonomously discovers, refines, and selects context-specific skills without human supervision or external feedback. At its core, a multi-agent self-play loop has a Challenger that generates probing tasks and rubrics, a Reasoner that attempts to solve them guided by an evolving skill set, and a neutral Judge that provides binary feedback. Crucially, both the Challenger and the Reasoner evolve through accumulated skills: dedicated Proposer and Generator agents analyze failure cases and synthesize them into targeted skill updates for both sides, enabling automated skill discovery and refinement. To prevent adversarial collapse caused by increasingly extreme task generation and over-specialized skill accumulation, we further introduce a Cross-time Replay mechanism that identifies the skill set achieving the best balance across representative cases for the Reasoner side, ensuring robust and generalizable skill evolution. The resulting skills can be plugged into any language model to obtain better context learning capability. Evaluated on four context learning tasks from CL-bench, Ctx2Skill consistently improves solving rates across backbone models.

</details>


### [42] [When Agents Evolve, Institutions Follow](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27691v1)
*Chao Fei,Hongcheng Guo,Yanghua Xiao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将历史政治制度转化为多agent架构，评估拓扑影响，强调自演化多agent系统，通用agent组织方法。

TL;DR: 历史政治制度为多智能体系统设计提供了结构化空间，不同治理拓扑导致集体性能差异显著，最优架构随模型和任务变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统面临类似历史上复杂社会的集体行动协调问题，其核心挑战在于集体组织而非个体智能，因此需要借鉴历史制度来探索有效架构。

Method: 将七种历史政治制度（四种治理模式）转化为可执行的多智能体架构，在三个大语言模型和两个基准测试中统一评估，分析治理拓扑对集体性能的影响。

Result: 治理拓扑强烈影响性能，同一模型内最佳与最差制度性能差距超过57个百分点；最优架构随模型能力和任务特征系统性地变化。

Conclusion: 集体智能的进步不依赖单一最优组织形式，而需要可重新选择和配置的治理机制，从而从自进化智能体转向自进化多智能体系统。

中文摘要：历经千年，复杂社会始终面临同样的协调问题：如何在认知有限、信息不完整的个体之间组织集体行动。不同文明发展出不同的政治制度来回答相同的基本问题：谁提议、谁审查、谁执行、以及如何纠正错误。我们提出，基于大语言模型的多智能体系统也面临同样的挑战。其核心问题不仅在于个体智能，更在于集体组织。因此，历史制度为多智能体架构提供了一个结构化的设计空间，使得效率与纠错、集中与分布、专业化与冗余之间的关键权衡得以经验性测试。我们将七种历史政治制度（涵盖四种典型治理模式）转化为可执行的多智能体架构，并在相同的条件下，跨三个大语言模型和两个基准测试进行评估。我们发现，治理拓扑强烈影响集体表现。在单一模型内，最佳与最差制度之间的差距超过57个百分点，而最优架构随模型能力和任务特征系统性变化。这些结果表明，集体智能不会通过单一最优组织形式进步，而是通过能够随任务和能力演变而重新选择和配置的治理机制。更广泛地说，这指向了从“自进化智能体”到“自进化多智能体系统”的转变。代码可在GitHub上获取。

Original abstract: Across millennia, complex societies have faced the same coordination problem of how to organize collective action among cognitively bounded and informationally incomplete individuals. Different civilizations developed different political institutions to answer the same basic questions of who proposes, who reviews, who executes, and how errors are corrected. We argue that multi-agent systems built on large language models face the same challenge. Their central problem is not only individual intelligence, but collective organization. Historical institutions therefore provide a structured design space for multi-agent architectures, making key trade-offs between efficiency and error correction, centralization and distribution, and specialization and redundancy empirically testable. We translate seven historical political institutions, spanning four canonical governance patterns, into executable multi-agent architectures and evaluate them under identical conditions across three large language models and two benchmarks. We find that governance topology strongly shapes collective performance. Within a single model, the gap between the best and worst institution exceeds 57 percentage points, while the optimal architecture shifts systematically with model capability and task characteristics. These results suggest that collective intelligence will not advance through a single optimal organizational form, but through governance mechanisms that can be reselected and reconfigured as tasks and capabilities evolve. More broadly, this points to a transition from \textbf{self-evolving agents} to the \textbf{self-evolving multi-agent system}. The code is available on \href{https://github.com/cf3i/SocialSystemArena}{GitHub}.

### [43] [Bridging Values and Behavior: A Hierarchical Framework for Proactive Embodied Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27699v1)
*Chunhui Zhang,Yuxuan Wang,Aoyang Qin,Yi-Long Lu,Kunlun Wu,Yizhou Wang,Wei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 具身agent分层认知架构ValuePlanner，结合LLM和PDDL规划，可迁移至coding agent规划。

TL;DR: ValuePlanner通过分层认知架构将价值调度与动作执行解耦，利用LLM生成子目标和PDDL规划器执行，实现自主代理的长期价值引导行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身代理缺乏稳定的高阶价值框架，无法支持长期自主行为和解决动机冲突。

Method: 提出ValuePlanner架构，使用LLM进行价值权衡生成符号子目标，再由PDDL规划器转化为动作计划，并通过闭环反馈优化。

Result: 在TongSim环境中，ValuePlanner相比基线的指令跟随和需求驱动方法，能生成更连贯的长期自主行为，并仲裁竞争价值。

Conclusion: ValuePlanner提供了一种结构化方法，将内在价值与具身行为桥接，为自主代理的价值驱动行为奠定基础。

中文摘要：当前的具身代理通常局限于被动的指令跟随或反应式的需求满足，缺乏一个稳定的高阶价值框架，这对于长期的自主行为和解决动机冲突至关重要。我们引入了ValuePlanner，一种分层认知架构，将高层价值调度与低层动作执行解耦。ValuePlanner采用基于LLM的认知模块，通过推理抽象的价值权衡来生成符号子目标，然后由经典的PDDL规划器将其转化为可执行的动作计划。这一过程通过闭环反馈机制进行优化。评估这样的自主性需要超越任务成功率的指标，因此我们提出了一套以价值为中心的评估套件，衡量累积价值增益、偏好对齐和行为多样性。在TongSim家庭环境中的实验表明，ValuePlanner能够仲裁相互竞争的价值，生成连贯的、长时域的自主行为，这是指令跟随和需求驱动基线所不具备的。我们的工作提供了一种结构化的方法，将内在价值与具身行为桥接起来，用于自主代理。

Original abstract: Current embodied agents are often limited to passive instruction-following or reactive need-satisfaction, lacking a stable, high-order value framework essential for long-term, self-directed behavior and resolving motivational conflicts. We introduce \textit{ValuePlanner}, a hierarchical cognitive architecture that decouples high-level value scheduling from low-level action execution. \textit{ValuePlanner} employs an LLM-based cognitive module to generate symbolic subgoals by reasoning through abstract value trade-offs, which are then translated into executable action plans by a classical PDDL planner. This process is refined via a closed-loop feedback mechanism. Evaluating such autonomy requires methods beyond task-success rates, and we therefore propose a value-centric evaluation suite measuring cumulative value gain, preference alignment, and behavioral diversity. Experiments in the TongSim household environment demonstrate that \textit{ValuePlanner} arbitrates competing values to generate coherent, long-horizon, self-directed behavior absent from instruction-following and needs-driven baselines. Our work offers a structured approach to bridging intrinsic values and grounded behavior for autonomous agents.

### [44] [Contextual Agentic Memory is a Memo, Not True Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27707v1)
*Binyan Xu,Xilin Dai,Kehuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 批判当前agent记忆为查找，提出记忆与学习分离，对agent长期学习设计有启发。

TL;DR: 当前AI记忆系统实为查找，而非真正记忆，导致泛化瓶颈和安全漏洞；借鉴神经科学，需结合快速存储与慢速巩固。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论证将查找视为记忆是范畴错误，并指出其对智能体能力、学习和安全性的后果。

Method: 形式化分析，借鉴互补学习系统理论，探讨替代观点。

Result: 识别出泛化上限和记忆中毒脆弱性，并指出当前系统只实现了生物记忆的一半。

Conclusion: 提出共存建议，并呼吁系统构建者、基准设计者和记忆社区采取行动。

中文摘要：当前智能体记忆系统（向量存储、检索增强生成、暂存器和上下文窗口管理）并未实现记忆：它们实现的是查找。我们认为，将查找视为记忆是一个范畴错误，会对智能体的能力、长期学习和安全性产生可证明的后果。检索通过相似性对存储案例进行泛化；基于权重的记忆通过将抽象规则应用于从未见过的输入进行泛化。将两者混为一谈会导致智能体无限积累笔记而无法发展专业知识，在组合新颖任务上面临可证明的泛化上限，该上限无法通过增加上下文大小或检索质量来克服，并且在结构上容易受到持久性记忆中毒的影响，因为注入的内容会传播到所有未来会话中。借鉴神经科学的互补学习系统理论，我们表明生物智能通过将快速的海马体示例存储与缓慢的新皮层权重巩固相结合来解决这个问题，而当前的AI智能体只实现了前一半。我们形式化了这些局限性，探讨了四种替代观点，并以共存建议和对系统构建者、基准设计者和记忆社区的行动呼吁作为结束。

Original abstract: Current agentic memory systems (vector stores, retrieval-augmented generation, scratchpads, and context-window management) do not implement memory: they implement lookup. We argue that treating lookup as memory is a category error with provable consequences for agent capability, long-term learning, and security. Retrieval generalizes by similarity to stored cases; weight-based memory generalizes by applying abstract rules to inputs never seen before. Conflating the two produces agents that accumulate notes indefinitely without developing expertise, face a provable generalization ceiling on compositionally novel tasks that no increase in context size or retrieval quality can overcome, and are structurally vulnerable to persistent memory poisoning as injected content propagates across all future sessions. Drawing on Complementary Learning Systems theory from neuroscience, we show that biological intelligence solved this problem by pairing fast hippocampal exemplar storage with slow neocortical weight consolidation, and that current AI agents implement only the first half. We formalize these limitations, address four alternative views, and close with a co-existence proposal and a call to action for system builders, benchmark designers, and the memory community.

</details>


### [45] [Knowledge Graph Representations for LLM-Based Policy Compliance Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27713v1)
*Wilder Baldwin,Sepideh Ghanavati*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 构建KG用于政策合规推理的agent框架，涉及检索与知识表示，对agent工具使用有参考。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出智能体框架，从政策文档构建知识图谱，使用两种本体模式，并评估五个LLM在42个QA任务上的表现。

Result: KG增强提升了所有五个模型的得分，LLM发现的本体模式匹配或超过形式化本体。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效，且灵活的本体发现方法优于预定义本体。

中文摘要：随着AI功能迅速集成到软件应用中，其带来的风险也在增加。为此，业界提出了安全可靠的AI法规和标准。在本文中，我们提出了一种智能体框架，该框架从AI政策文档中构建知识图谱（KG），并检索与政策相关的信息来回答问题。我们根据两种本体模式从三项AI风险相关政策中构建了知识图谱，然后使用启发式评分和LLM作为评判者，对五个LLM在42个涵盖六种推理类型（从实体查找到跨政策推理）的政策问答任务上进行了评估。知识图谱增强提升了所有五个模型的得分，并且一个开放的、由LLM发现的模式匹配或超过了形式化本体。

Original abstract: The risks posed by AI features are increasing as they are rapidly integrated into software applications. In response, regulations and standards for safe and secure AI have been proposed. In this paper, we present an agentic framework that constructs knowledge graphs (KGs) from AI policy documents and retrieves policy-relevant information to answer questions. We build KGs from three AI risk-related polices under two ontology schemas, and then evaluate five LLMs on 42 policy QA tasks spanning six reasoning types, from entity lookup to cross-policy inference, using both heuristic scoring and an LLM-as-judge. KG augmentation improves scores for all five models, and an open, LLM-discovered schema matches or exceeds the formal ontology.

### [46] [Iterative Multimodal Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Medical Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27724v1)
*Xupeng Chen,Binbin Shi,Chenqian Le,Jiaqi Zhang,Kewen Wang,Ran Gong,Jinhan Zhang,Chihang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 迭代多模态RAG框架，可视为agent检索与推理组件，但未涉及agent规划或执行。

TL;DR: 提出MED-VRAG，一种基于PMC页面图像的多模态RAG框架，通过迭代检索和视觉语言推理，在医学QA上达到78.6%准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学RAG系统仅使用文本块，丢弃了表格、图形等视觉信息，限制了理解能力。

Method: MED-VRAG采用ColQwen2.5对页面图像进行补丁级嵌入，通过粗到细索引（C=8质心/页+ANN）实现快速检索，并用MapReduce LLM过滤；然后使用VLM进行最多3轮迭代推理，每轮优化查询并在记忆库中积累证据。

Result: 在4个医学QA基准上平均准确率78.6%，检索贡献+5.8%，优于无检索基线；消融显示页面图像+1.0%、迭代+1.5%、记忆库+1.0%。

Conclusion: 利用页面图像替代文本块能显著提升医学RAG性能，迭代推理和记忆库进一步带来增益。

中文摘要：医学检索增强生成（RAG）系统通常操作从生物医学文献中提取的文本块，丢弃了原始文档页面的丰富视觉内容（表格、图形、结构化布局）。我们提出MED-VRAG，一个迭代的多模态RAG框架，它检索并推理PMC文档页面图像，而不是OCR文本。该系统将ColQwen2.5补丁级页面嵌入与分片MapReduce LLM过滤器配对，通过离线粗到细索引（每页C=8个质心，质心的ANN，对顶部R候选进行精确双向评分）扩展到约35万页，同时将第一阶段检索控制在30毫秒以下。视觉语言模型（VLM）然后迭代地优化其查询，并在最多3轮推理中在记忆库中积累证据，单次迭代在4个A100上花费约15.9秒，完整的3轮流程约47.8秒。在四个医学问答基准（MedQA、MedMCQA、PubMedQA、MMLU-Med）上，MED-VRAG达到了78.6%的平均准确率。在与相同Qwen2.5-VL-32B主干网络的控制比较下，检索相对于无检索基线贡献了+5.8个百分点的增益；我们还注意到相对于MedRAG + GPT-4（76.8%）有+1.8个百分点的优势，但需要注意这是跨论文比较，并非直接对比。消融实验分别分离了页面图像与文本块检索带来的+1.0、迭代带来的+1.5以及记忆库带来的+1.0。

Original abstract: Medical retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically operate on text chunks extracted from biomedical literature, discarding the rich visual content (tables, figures, structured layouts) of original document pages. We propose MED-VRAG, an iterative multimodal RAG framework that retrieves and reasons over PMC document page images instead of OCR'd text. The system pairs ColQwen2.5 patch-level page embeddings with a sharded MapReduce LLM filter, scaling to ~350K pages while keeping Stage-1 retrieval under 30 ms via an offline coarse-to-fine index (C=8 centroids per page, ANN over centroids, exact two-way scoring on the top-R shortlist). A vision-language model (VLM) then iteratively refines its query and accumulates evidence in a memory bank across up to 3 reasoning rounds, with a single iteration costing ~15.9 s and the full three-round pipeline ~47.8 s on 4xA100. Across four medical QA benchmarks (MedQA, MedMCQA, PubMedQA, MMLU-Med), MEDVRAG reaches 78.6% average accuracy. Under controlled comparison with the same Qwen2.5-VL-32B backbone, retrieval contributes a +5.8 point gain over the no-retrieval baseline; we also note a +1.8 point edge over MedRAG + GPT-4 (76.8%), with the caveat that this is a cross-paper rather than head-to-head comparison. Ablations isolate +1.0 from page-image vs text-chunk retrieval, +1.5 from iteration, and +1.0 from the memory bank.

### [47] [WindowsWorld: A Process-Centric Benchmark of Autonomous GUI Agents in Professional Cross-Application Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27776v1)
*Jinchao Li,Yunxin Li,Chenrui Zhao,Zhenran Xu,Baotian Hu,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 跨应用GUI agent benchmark，涉及长程多步任务，可迁移至coding agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出WindowsWorld基准，测试GUI代理在跨应用程序工作流程上的表现，发现代理在多应用任务上成功率低、推理能力差、效率低下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基准忽略跨应用工作流程，需要评估代理在真实多步骤专业任务上的能力。

Method: 使用多代理框架（16个职业驱动）生成四个难度级别的任务，经人工审核后在模拟环境执行，最终181个任务，78%多应用。

Result: 所有代理在多应用任务成功率<21%，跨≥3应用任务失败，步骤限制下仍低效。

Conclusion: 现有GUI代理在多应用复杂工作流程中表现不足，需要进一步改进。

中文摘要：虽然GUI代理在常见的计算机使用任务（如OSWorld）中展示了令人印象深刻的能力，但当前的基准测试主要集中在孤立和单一应用任务上。这忽略了跨多个应用程序协调以完成复杂的专业特定工作流程的关键现实需求。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了一个跨应用程序工作流程的计算机使用基准，名为WindowsWorld，旨在系统地评估GUI代理在复杂的多步骤任务中的表现，这些任务反映了真实的专业活动。我们的方法使用一个由16个职业驱动的多代理框架来生成四个难度级别的任务，并带有中间检查点，然后通过人工审查进行细化，并在模拟环境中执行。生成的基准包含181个任务，平均每个任务有5.0个子目标，涵盖17个常见桌面应用程序，其中78%本质上是多应用程序的。对领先的大模型和代理的实验结果表明：1）所有计算机使用代理在多应用程序任务上表现不佳（成功率<21%），远低于简单单应用任务的表现；2）它们大多无法完成需要条件判断和跨≥3个应用程序推理的任务，在早期子目标处停滞；3）执行效率低下，任务经常失败，尽管远远超过了人类步骤限制。代码、基准数据和评估资源可在github.com/HITsz-TMG/WindowsWorld获取。

Original abstract: While GUI agents have shown impressive capabilities in common computer-use tasks such as OSWorld, current benchmarks mainly focus on isolated and single-application tasks. This overlooks a critical real-world requirement of coordinating across multiple applications to accomplish complex profession-specific workflows. To bridge this gap, we present a computer-use benchmark in cross-application workflows, named WindowsWorld, designed to systematically assess GUI Agents on complex multi-step tasks that mirror real-world professional activities. Our methodology uses a multi-agent framework steered by 16 occupations to generate four difficulty-level tasks with intermediate inspection, which are then refined by human review and executed in a simulated environment. The resulting benchmark contains 181 tasks with an average of 5.0 sub-goals across 17 common desktop applications, of which 78% are inherently multi-application. Experimental results of leading large models and agents show that: 1) All computer-use agents perform poorly on multi-application tasks (< 21% success rate), far below the performance of simple single-app tasks; 2) They largely fail at tasks requiring conditional judgment and reasoning across $\geq$ 3 applications, stalling at early sub-goals; 3) Low execution efficiency, where tasks often fail despite far exceeding human step limits. Code, benchmark data, and evaluation resources are available at github.com/HITsz-TMG/WindowsWorld.

### [48] [AgentReputation: A Decentralized Agentic AI Reputation Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00073v1)
*Mohd Sameen Chishti,Damilare Peter Oyinloye,Jingyue Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了三层信誉框架AgentReputation，将任务执行、信誉服务和防篡改持久化分离；引入显式验证机制和上下文条件信誉卡以防混淆；提供面向决策的策略引擎支持资源分配、访问控制和自适应验证升级。

Result: 框架实现了信誉管理的去中心化，分离了不同关注点，并提供了基于风险和不确定性的自适应验证机制。

Conclusion: 未来研究方向包括验证本体开发、验证强度量化、隐私保护证据、冷启动信誉引导和对抗操纵防御。

中文摘要：去中心化的智能体AI市场正在迅速涌现，以支持调试、补丁生成和安全审计等软件工程任务，这些市场通常在没有中央监督的情况下运行。然而，现有的信誉机制在这种环境下因三个根本原因而失效：智能体可以战略性地优化以对抗评估程序；展示的能力不能可靠地跨异构任务上下文转移；以及验证的严格程度差异很大，从轻量级自动检查到昂贵的专家审查。当前基于联邦学习、区块链AI平台和大语言模型安全研究的信誉方法无法综合应对这些挑战。因此，我们提出了AgentReputation，一种用于智能体AI系统的去中心化三层信誉框架。该框架将任务执行、信誉服务和防篡改持久化分离，以利用各自的优势并实现独立演化。该框架引入了与智能体信誉元数据关联的显式验证机制，以及防止跨域和任务类型信誉混淆的上下文条件信誉卡。此外，AgentReputation提供了一个面向决策的策略引擎，支持基于风险和不确定性的资源分配、访问控制和自适应验证升级。基于此框架，我们概述了几个未来研究方向，包括验证本体开发、验证强度量化方法、隐私保护证据机制、冷启动信誉引导以及对抗操纵的防御。

Original abstract: Decentralized, agentic AI marketplaces are rapidly emerging to support software engineering tasks such as debugging, patch generation, and security auditing, often operating without centralized oversight. However, existing reputation mechanisms fail in this setting for three fundamental reasons: agents can strategically optimize against evaluation procedures; demonstrated competence does not reliably transfer across heterogeneous task contexts; and verification rigor varies widely, from lightweight automated checks to costly expert review. Current approaches to reputation drawing on federated learning, blockchain-based AI platforms, and large language model safety research are unable to address these challenges in combination. We therefore propose \textbf{AgentReputation}, a decentralized, three-layer reputation framework for agentic AI systems. The framework separates task execution, reputation services, and tamper-proof persistence to both leverage their respective strengths and enable independent evolution. The framework introduces explicit verification regimes linked to agent reputation metadata, as well as context-conditioned reputation cards that prevent reputation conflation across domains and task types. In addition, AgentReputation provides a decision-facing policy engine that supports resource allocation, access control, and adaptive verification escalation based on risk and uncertainty. Building on this framework, we outline several future research directions, including the development of verification ontologies, methods for quantifying verification strength, privacy-preserving evidence mechanisms, cold-start reputation bootstrapping, and defenses against adversarial manipulation.

### [49] [MCPHunt: An Evaluation Framework for Cross-Boundary Data Propagation in Multi-Server MCP Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27819v1)
*Haonan Li,Tianjun Sun,Yongqing Wang,Qisheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: MCP agent跨边界数据传播评估，涉及agent安全与信息流控制。

TL;DR: 提出MCPHunt基准测试，揭示多服务器MCP代理中非恶意的凭证传播问题，传播率高达41.3%，提示缓解虽有效但存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多服务器MCP代理中，工具组合可能导致良性权限跨边界传播凭证，构成信息流控制难题。

Method: 设计MCPHunt基准，包括金丝雀污点跟踪、环境控制覆盖设计和CRS分层，以隔离并量化非对抗性凭证传播。

Result: 在5个模型上测得11.5%-41.3%的违反策略传播率，传播路径特异性强，集中于浏览器数据流；提示缓解可将传播率降低97%但效用保留80.5%，且效果随指令遵循能力变化。

Conclusion: 提示级防御可能不足，需更 robust 的机制；已开源全部代码和数据。

中文摘要：多服务器MCP代理造成了信息流控制问题：忠实的工具组合可以将个体上良性的读/写权限转化为跨边界凭证传播——这是工作流拓扑的结构性副作用，不一定是模型恶意行为。我们提出了MCPHunt，据我们所知，这是第一个隔离跨多服务器MCP信任边界的非对抗性、逐字凭证传播的受控基准，包含三项方法论贡献：（1）基于金丝雀的污点跟踪，将传播检测简化为客观字符串匹配；（2）环境控制的覆盖设计，包含风险、良性和硬负例条件，验证流水线合理性并控制凭证格式混淆；（3）CRS分层，将任务强制传播（忠实执行逐字传输指令）与违反策略的传播（尽管有删除选项但仍包含凭证）区分开来。在来自5个模型、涵盖147个任务和9种机制家族的3,615条主要基准轨迹中，所有模型的违反策略传播率达到11.5%至41.3%。这种传播具有路径特异性（跨机制范围达25倍），并集中在浏览器介导的数据流中；硬负例控制证据表明，生产格式凭证并非必要——提示导向的跨边界数据流就足够了。对3个模型的提示缓解研究将违反策略的传播减少了高达97%，同时保留了80.5%的效用，但效果因指令遵循能力而异——表明仅凭提示级别的防御可能不足。代码、轨迹和标注流水线以MIT和CC BY 4.0许可发布。

Original abstract: Multi-server MCP agents create an information-flow control problem: faithful tool composition can turn individually benign read/write permissions into cross-boundary credential propagation -- a structural side effect of workflow topology, not necessarily malicious model behavior. We present MCPHunt, to our knowledge the first controlled benchmark that isolates non-adversarial, verbatim credential propagation across multi-server MCP trust boundaries, with three methodological contributions: (1) canary-based taint tracking that reduces propagation detection to objective string matching; (2) an environment-controlled coverage design with risky, benign, and hard-negative conditions that validates pipeline soundness and controls for credential-format confounds; (3) CRS stratification that disentangles task-mandated propagation (faithful execution of verbatim-transfer instructions) from policy-violating propagation (credentials included despite the option to redact). Across 3,615 main-benchmark traces from 5 models spanning 147 tasks and 9 mechanism families, policy-violating propagation rates reach 11.5--41.3% across all models. This propagation is pathway-specific (25x cross-mechanism range) and concentrated in browser-mediated data flows; hard-negative controls provide evidence that production-format credentials are not necessary -- prompt-directed cross-boundary data flow is sufficient. A prompt-mitigation study across 3 models reduces policy-violating propagation by up to 97% while preserving 80.5% utility, but effectiveness varies with instruction-following capability -- suggesting that prompt-level defenses alone may not suffice. Code, traces, and labeling pipeline are released under MIT and CC BY 4.0.

</details>


### [50] [ObjectGraph: From Document Injection to Knowledge Traversal -- A Native File Format for the Agentic Era](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27820v1)
*Mohit Dubey,Open Gigantic*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 新文件格式减少agent token消耗，可直接提升coding agent效率。

TL;DR: 提出OBJECTGRAPH格式，将文档视为知识图谱而非字符串，显著减少LLM代理的令牌消耗而不损失任务准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文档格式为人类线性阅读设计，与LLM代理的检索方式不匹配，导致令牌浪费、状态累积和信息广播问题，且非提示工程、检索或压缩问题，而是格式问题。

Method: 引入OBJECTGRAPH格式，基于类型化有向知识图谱，是Markdown超集，支持两原语查询协议；形式化文档消费问题并证明满足六个结构属性；提出渐进式披露模型、角色限定访问协议和可执行断言节点。

Result: 在五个文档类别和八种代理任务上，令牌减少高达95.3%，任务准确率无统计学显著下降（p > 0.05），转译器保真度达98.7%。

Conclusion: OBJECTGRAPH作为一种新格式，有效解决了LLM代理与文档格式的失配问题，大幅降低令牌消耗且保持任务性能。

中文摘要：现存的每一种文档格式都是为人类读者线性阅读文本而设计的。自主LLM代理不阅读——它们检索。这一根本性不匹配迫使代理将整个文档注入其上下文窗口，在无关内容上浪费令牌，在多轮循环中累积状态，并在代理角色之间不加区分地广播信息。我们认为这不是一个提示工程问题，不是检索问题，也不是压缩问题：这是一个格式问题。
我们引入了OBJECTGRAPH（.og），一种文件格式，它将文档重新构想为一种带类型的、有向的知识图谱以供遍历，而不是一个需要注入的字符串。OBJECTGRAPH是Markdown的严格超集——每个.md文件都是一个有效的.og文件——除了一个两原语查询协议外不需要任何基础设施，并且无需工具即可被人类和代理读取。
我们形式化了文档消费问题，描述了现有格式无法同时满足的六个结构属性，并证明了OBJECTGRAPH满足所有六个属性。我们进一步引入了渐进式披露模型、角色限定访问协议和可执行断言节点作为原生格式原语。在五个文档类别和八种代理任务类型上的实证评估显示，令牌减少高达95.3%，且任务准确率无统计学显著下降（p > 0.05）。转译器保真度在保留的文档基准上达到98.7%的内容保存。

Original abstract: Every document format in existence was designed for a human reader moving linearly through text. Autonomous LLM agents do not read - they retrieve. This fundamental mismatch forces agents to inject entire documents into their context window, wasting tokens on irrelevant content, compounding state across multi-turn loops, and broadcasting information indiscriminately across agent roles. We argue this is not a prompt engineering problem, not a retrieval problem, and not a compression problem: it is a format problem.
  We introduce OBJECTGRAPH (.og), a file format that reconceives the document as a typed, directed knowledge graph to be traversed rather than a string to be injected. OBJECTGRAPH is a strict superset of Markdown - every .md file is a valid .og file - requires no infrastructure beyond a two-primitive query protocol, and is readable by both humans and agents without tooling.
  We formalize the Document Consumption Problem, characterise six structural properties no existing format satisfies simultaneously, and prove OBJECTGRAPH satisfies all six. We further introduce the Progressive Disclosure Model, the Role-Scoped Access Protocol, and Executable Assertion Nodes as native format primitives. Empirical evaluation across five document classes and eight agent task types demonstrates up to 95.3 percent token reduction with no statistically significant degradation in task accuracy (p > 0.05). Transpiler fidelity reaches 98.7 percent content preservation on a held-out document benchmark.

</details>


### [51] [Rethinking Agentic Reinforcement Learning In Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27859v3)
*Fangming Cui,Ruixiao Zhu,Cheng Fang,Sunan Li,Jiahong Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agentic RL概念与设计，直接指导agent训练方法。

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于大语言模型的智能体强化学习范式，探讨其概念基础、方法创新、挑战与未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RL局限于静态目标和简单环境，而LLM的出现推动了向能够自主设定目标、长期规划和动态适应的智能体RL范式转变。

Method: 通过分析基于LLM的智能体RL的概念基础、方法创新和有效设计，包括元推理、自我反思和多步决策等认知能力的整合。

Result: 识别了该领域的关键挑战，并概述了未来有前景的研究方向。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的智能体RL代表了RL领域的重要范式转变，通过融入类似认知的能力，为构建更自主、适应性更强的智能体提供了新路径，但仍面临诸多挑战需要进一步研究。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）传统上专注于训练专门的智能体，以在狭窄定义的环境中优化预定义的奖励函数。然而，强大的大语言模型（LLM）和日益复杂、开放式任务的出现，催化了RL向智能体范式的转变。这一新兴框架超越了传统RL，强调发展能够设定目标、长期规划、动态策略调整以及在不确定的真实世界环境中进行交互推理的自主智能体。与依赖静态目标和间歇性交互的传统方法不同，基于LLM的智能体RL将元推理、自我反思和多步决策等类似认知的能力直接纳入学习循环中。在本文中，我们深入探讨了这一趋势背后的概念基础、方法创新和有效设计。此外，我们识别了关键挑战，并概述了构建基于LLM的智能体RL的未来有前景的方向。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has traditionally focused on training specialized agents to optimize predefined reward functions within narrowly defined environments. However, the advent of powerful Large Language Models (LLMs) and increasingly complex, open-ended tasks has catalyzed a paradigm shift towards agentic paradigms within RL. This emerging framework extends beyond traditional RL by emphasizing the development of autonomous agents capable of goal-setting, long-term planning, dynamic strategy adaptation, and interactive reasoning in uncertain, real-world environments. Unlike conventional approaches that rely heavily on static objectives and episodic interactions, LLM-based Agentic RL incorporates cognitive-like capabilities such as meta-reasoning, self-reflection, and multi-step decision-making directly into the learning loop. In this paper, we provide a deep insight for looking the conceptual foundations, methodological innovations, and effective designs underlying this trend. Furthermore, we identify critical challenges and outline promising future directions for building LLM-based Agentic RL.

### [52] [KellyBench: A Benchmark for Long-Horizon Sequential Decision Making](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27865v1)
*Thomas Grady,Kip Parker,Iliyan Zarov,Henry Course,Chengxi Taylor,Ross Taylor*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长程决策benchmark，评估agent规划适应能力，可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 本文提出KellyBench，一个评估体育博彩序列决策的环境，发现前沿模型均亏损，表现最好的模型平均回报-8%，且策略复杂度远低于人类专家。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型在程序性任务上表现饱和，但它们在长期、非平稳、开放式目标环境中的决策能力尚未得到充分评估，因此需要更实际、动态的基准来测试其序列决策能力。

Method: 构建KellyBench环境，模拟2023-24赛季英超联赛的体育博彩市场，提供详细历史数据（高级统计、阵容、赔率），要求智能体构建模型、识别市场优势并适应环境变化，使用人类专家评分标准评估策略。

Conclusion: 当前语言模型在长期序列决策任务中表现不佳，存在显著改进空间，KellyBench为此类任务提供了有效的评估平台。

中文摘要：语言模型在具有狭窄目标的程序性任务的基准测试中正在趋于饱和。但它们正越来越多地被部署在具有开放式目标的长期、非平稳环境中。在本文中，我们介绍了KellyBench，一个用于评估体育博彩市场中序列决策的环境。智能体被置于2023-24赛季英格兰足球超级联赛的序列模拟中，任务是最大化其长期资金增长。它们被提供详细的历史数据，包括高级统计、阵容和公开赔率。为了成功，它们必须构建机器学习模型，识别公开市场中的优势，并随着环境随时间变化而适应。我们发现，所有评估的前沿模型在五个种子上平均在整个赛季中亏损。表现最好的模型实现了平均-8%的回报，许多模型在不同种子中遭遇破产。为了判断策略的复杂性，我们使用人类专家评分标准对每个模型进行评分，发现它们的方法与人类基线相比不够复杂；Claude Opus 4.6的评分得分为26.5%，这意味着还有很大的改进空间。KellyBench可作为开放访问API端点使用，网址为https://openreward.ai/GeneralReasoning/KellyBench。

Original abstract: Language models are saturating benchmarks for procedural tasks with narrow objectives. But they are increasingly being deployed in long-horizon, non-stationary environments with open-ended goals. In this paper we introduce KellyBench, an environment for evaluating sequential decision-making in sports betting markets. Agents are placed in a sequential simulation of the 2023-24 English Premier League season and tasked with maximising their long-term bankroll growth. They are given detailed historical data, including advanced statistics, lineups, and public odds. To succeed they must build machine learning models, identify edge in public markets, and adapt as the environment changes over time. We find that all frontier models evaluated lose money on average over the course of the season for five seeds. The best performing model achieves an average return of -8%, and many models experiencing ruin across seeds. To judge strategy sophistication, we use a human expert rubric to grade each model and find their approaches to be unsophisticated compared to human baselines; Claude Opus 4.6 achieves a rubric score of 26.5%, which means there is significant room for improvement. KellyBench is available as an open-access API endpoint at https://openreward.ai/GeneralReasoning/KellyBench.

Original abstract: Recent advances in agentic AI are shifting automation from discrete tools to proactive multi-agent systems that coordinate multi-specialized capabilities behind unified interfaces. Given this limitation, we argue that on-demand persona-based agent generation offers a promising path towards more efficient and contextually appropriate interaction within agentic workflows. By dynamically crafting agents and personas at run-time to match user characteristics, task demands, and workflow context, agentic platforms can move beyond one-size-fits-all configurations. ### [54] [In-Context Prompting Obsoletes Agent Orchestration for Procedural Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27891v2)
*Simon Dennis,Michael Diamond,Rivaan Patil,Kevin Shabahang,Hao Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 比较in-context prompting vs外部编排，对agent架构设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: 对于程序性任务，将整个程序放入系统提示让模型自我编排，优于使用外部编排框架（如LangGraph）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理编排框架在LLM之上增加外部编排器，但可能对于现代模型而言过于复杂，因此希望探索更简单的替代方案是否表现更好。

Method: 在旅行预订、Zoom技术支持、保险理赔三个领域，分别使用上下文方法（系统提示包含完整程序）和LangGraph编排器，每条件200次对话，用LLM-as-judge评分。

Result: 上下文方法在5分制得分4.53-5.00，失败率0.5%-11.5%；LangGraph编排器得分4.17-4.84，失败率9%-24%。

Conclusion: 对于遵循定义程序的多轮对话，外部编排不再必要，前沿模型能力已足以自我编排。

中文摘要：代理编排框架——如LangGraph、CrewAI、Google ADK、OpenAI Agents SDK等——将外部编排器置于LLM之上，每一步都跟踪状态并注入路由指令。我们通过受控比较表明，对于程序性任务，这种架构被一种更简单的替代方案所超越：将整个程序放在系统提示中，让模型自我编排。在三个领域——旅行预订（14个节点）、Zoom技术支持（14个节点）和保险理赔处理（55个节点）——我们使用LLM-as-judge评分对五个质量标准评估每个条件下200次对话。上下文方法在5分制上得分为4.53-5.00，而使用相同模型的LangGraph编排器得分为4.17-4.84。编排系统在24%的旅行、9%的Zoom和17%的保险对话中失败，而上下文基线分别为11.5%、0.5%和5%。虽然外部编排对于早期模型可能是必要的，但前沿模型能力的进步使其对于遵循定义程序的多轮对话变得不必要。

Original abstract: Agent orchestration frameworks -- LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, and others -- place an external orchestrator above the LLM, tracking state and injecting routing instructions at every turn. We present a controlled comparison showing that for procedural tasks, this architecture is dominated by a simpler alternative: putting the entire procedure in the system prompt and letting the model self-orchestrate. Across three domains -- travel booking (14 nodes), Zoom technical support (14 nodes), and insurance claims processing (55 nodes) -- we evaluate 200 conversations per condition using LLM-as-judge scoring on five quality criteria. The in-context approach scores 4.53--5.00 on a 5-point scale while a LangGraph orchestrator using the same model scores 4.17--4.84. The orchestrated system fails on 24% of travel, 9% of Zoom, and 17% of insurance conversations, compared to 11.5%, 0.5%, and 5% for the in-context baseline. While external orchestration may have been necessary for earlier models, advances in frontier model capabilities have made it unnecessary for multi-turn conversations following a defined procedure.

### [55] [Graph World Models: Concepts, Taxonomy, and Future Directions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27895v1)
*Jiawei Liu,Senqiao Yang,Mingjun Wang,Yu Wang,Bei Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 图世界模型作为agent环境建模基础，可用于规划与推理，值得跟踪。

TL;DR: 本文系统定义了图世界模型（GWM）的概念，并基于关系归纳偏置提出了一个分类法，将现有工作分为空间、物理和逻辑三类，并总结了设计原则、代表性模型和未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典世界模型基于平面张量，存在噪声敏感、误差累积和推理弱的问题，而基于图结构的方法能够分解环境为实体和交互，但缺乏统一的形式化和综述。

Method: 通过系统性形式化将基于图的世界模型统一为图世界模型（GWM），并提出基于关系归纳偏置（RIB）的分类法，分为空间RIB、物理RIB和逻辑RIB三类，并分析每类的设计原则和代表性模型。

Result: 提出了GWM的统一框架和RIB分类法，总结了空间、物理、逻辑三类模型的设计要点，并进行了比较分析。

Conclusion: GWM是一个有前景的研究范式，未来需要解决动态图适应、概率关系动态、多粒度归纳偏置以及专用基准和评估指标等挑战。

中文摘要：作为人工智能的主流模型之一，世界模型允许智能体学习环境的表示以进行高效的预测和规划。然而，基于平面张量的经典世界模型面临几个关键问题，包括噪声敏感性、误差累积和推理能力弱。为了解决这些局限性，许多最近的研究使用图结构将环境分解为实体节点和交互边，并在结构化空间中建模虚拟环境。本文系统地将这些新兴的基于图的工作形式化并统一到图世界模型（GWM）的概念下。据我们所知，GWM尚未被明确地定义和综述为一个统一的研究范式。此外，我们提出了一种基于关系归纳偏置（RIB）的分类法，根据GWM注入的特定结构先验对其进行分类：（1）用于拓扑抽象的空间RIB；（2）用于动态模拟的物理RIB；（3）用于因果和语义推理的逻辑RIB。对于每一类模型，我们概述了关键的设计原则，总结了代表性模型，并进行了比较分析。我们进一步讨论了开放挑战和未来方向，包括动态图适应、概率关系动态、多粒度归纳偏置，以及为GWM提供专用基准和评估指标的需求。

Original abstract: As one of the mainstream models of artificial intelligence, world models allow agents to learn the representation of the environment for efficient prediction and planning. However, classical world models based on flat tensors face several key problems, including noise sensitivity, error accumulation and weak reasoning. To address these limitations, many recent studies use graph structure to decompose the environment into entity nodes and interactive edges, and model virtual environments in a structured space. This paper systematically formalizes and unifies these emerging graph-based works under the concept of graph world models (GWMs). To the best of our knowledge, GWMs have not yet been explicitly defined and surveyed as a unified research paradigm. Furthermore, we propose a taxonomy based on relational inductive biases (RIB), categorizing GWMs by the specific structural priors they inject: (1) spatial RIB for topological abstraction; (2) physical RIB for dynamic simulation; and (3) logical RIB for causal and semantic reasoning. For each model category, we outline the key design principles, summarize representative models, and conduct comparative analyses. We further discuss open challenges and future directions, including dynamic graph adaptation, probabilistic relational dynamics, multi-granularity inductive biases, and the need for dedicated benchmarks and evaluation metrics for GWMs.

### [56] [From Unstructured Recall to Schema-Grounded Memory: Reliable AI Memory via Iterative, Schema-Aware Extraction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27906v2)
*Alex Petrov,Alexander Gusak,Denis Mukha,Dima Korolev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于schema的agent记忆架构，迭代提取与验证，对agent记忆模块设计有重要参考。

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于模式（schema）的AI外部记忆系统，通过将记忆摄入分解为对象检测、字段检测和字段值提取，并引入验证和重试机制，将解释从读取路径转移到写入路径，显著提升了结构化事实记忆的准确性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI记忆系统将记忆简化为检索问题，适用于主题回忆但不适合需要确切事实、状态更新、聚合、关系等操作的生产环境，缺乏对精确事实和状态化计算的支持。

Method: 提出基于模式（schema）的记忆架构，设计迭代的写入路径：将记忆摄入分为对象检测、字段检测和字段值提取，并引入验证门、本地重试和有状态提示控制，将解释从读取路径转移到写入路径。

Result: 在结构化提取基准上达到90.42%对象级准确率和62.67%输出准确率，在端到端记忆基准上达到97.10% F1，在应用级任务上达到95.2%准确率，均优于对比基线。

Conclusion: 对于需要稳定事实和有状态计算的记忆工作负载，架构设计比检索规模或模型强度更重要，基于模式的写入路径能显著提升记忆系统的可靠性。

中文摘要：持久的人工智能记忆通常被简化为一个检索问题：将先前的交互存储为文本，嵌入它们，并要求模型稍后恢复相关上下文。这种设计对于主题回忆很有用，但它与代理在生产中需要的记忆类型不匹配：确切的事实、当前状态、更新和删除、聚合、关系、否定查询以及明确的未知。这些操作要求记忆的行为更像一个记录系统，而不是搜索。
本文论证了可靠的外部人工智能记忆必须基于模式（schema）构建。模式定义了必须记住什么、可以忽略什么以及哪些值绝不能推断。我们提出了一种迭代的、模式感知的写入路径，将记忆摄入分解为对象检测、字段检测和字段值提取，并带有验证门、本地重试和有状态的提示控制。结果将解释从读取路径转移到写入路径：读取成为对已验证记录的有约束查询，而不是对检索到的散文进行重复推理。
我们在结构化提取和端到端记忆基准测试上评估了这种设计。在提取基准测试中，循环中的判断配置达到了90.42%的对象级准确率和62.67%的输出准确率，高于所有测试的前沿结构化输出基线。在端到端记忆基准测试中，xmemory达到了97.10%的F1分数，而第三方基线在80.16%-87.24%之间。在应用级任务上，xmemory达到了95.2%的准确率，优于专门的记忆系统、代码生成的Markdown工具和面向客户的前沿模型应用工具。结果表明，对于需要稳定事实和有状态计算的记忆工作负载，架构比检索规模或模型强度本身更重要。

Original abstract: Persistent AI memory is often reduced to a retrieval problem: store prior interactions as text, embed them, and ask the model to recover relevant context later. This design is useful for thematic recall, but it is mismatched to the kinds of memory that agents need in production: exact facts, current state, updates and deletions, aggregation, relations, negative queries, and explicit unknowns. These operations require memory to behave less like search and more like a system of record.
  This paper argues that reliable external AI memory must be schema-grounded. Schemas define what must be remembered, what may be ignored, and which values must never be inferred. We present an iterative, schema-aware write path that decomposes memory ingestion into object detection, field detection, and field-value extraction, with validation gates, local retries, and stateful prompt control. The result shifts interpretation from the read path to the write path: reads become constrained queries over verified records rather than repeated inference over retrieved prose.
  We evaluate this design on structured extraction and end-to-end memory benchmarks. On the extraction benchmark, the judge-in-the-loop configuration reaches 90.42% object-level accuracy and 62.67% output accuracy, above all tested frontier structured-output baselines. On our end-to-end memory benchmark, xmemory reaches 97.10% F1, compared with 80.16%-87.24% across the third-party baselines. On the application-level task, xmemory reaches 95.2% accuracy, outperforming specialised memory systems, code-generated Markdown harnesses, and customer-facing frontier-model application harnesses. The results show that, for memory workloads requiring stable facts and stateful computation, architecture matters more than retrieval scale or model strength alone.

</details>


### [57] [MM-StanceDet: Retrieval-Augmented Multi-modal Multi-agent Stance Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27934v1)
*Weihai Lu,Zhejun Zhao,Yanshu Li,Huan He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent框架融合检索增强与自我反思，可迁移到coding agent中的多agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出 MM-StanceDet，一种检索增强的多智能体框架，通过上下文基础、多模态分析、推理增强辩论和自我反思阶段，显著提升多模态立场检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MSD方法在上下文基础、跨模态解释和单次推理方面存在不足，难以处理文本和图像冲突信号。

Method: 提出检索增强的多模态多智能体框架MM-StanceDet，包含检索增强上下文基础、专门多模态分析智能体、推理增强辩论阶段和自反思裁决。

Result: 在五个数据集上显著优于最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: 多智能体架构和结构化推理阶段能有效应对复杂多模态立场挑战。

中文摘要：多模态立场检测（MSD）对于理解公共话语至关重要，然而有效融合文本和图像（尤其是在存在冲突信号的情况下）仍然具有挑战性。现有方法常常面临上下文基础不足、跨模态解释歧义以及单次推理脆弱性等问题。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了检索增强的多模态多智能体立场检测（MM-StanceDet），这是一种新颖的多智能体框架，集成了用于上下文基础的检索增强、用于细致解释的专门多模态分析智能体、用于探索视角的推理增强辩论阶段以及用于稳健裁决的自我反思。在五个数据集上的大量实验表明，MM-StanceDet显著优于最先进的基线，验证了其多智能体架构和结构化推理阶段在应对复杂多模态立场挑战方面的有效性。

Original abstract: Multimodal Stance Detection (MSD) is crucial for understanding public discourse, yet effectively fusing text and image, especially with conflicting signals, remains challenging. Existing methods often face difficulties with contextual grounding, cross-modal interpretation ambiguity, and single-pass reasoning fragility. To address these, we propose Retrieval-Augmented Multi-modal Multi-agent Stance Detection (MM-StanceDet), a novel multi-agent framework integrating Retrieval Augmentation for contextual grounding, specialized Multimodal Analysis agents for nuanced interpretation, a Reasoning-Enhanced Debate stage for exploring perspectives, and Self-Reflection for robust adjudication. Extensive experiments on five datasets demonstrate MM-StanceDet significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, validating the efficacy of its multi-agent architecture and structured reasoning stages in addressing complex multimodal stance challenges.

### [58] [The Effects of Visual Priming on Cooperative Behavior in Vision-Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27953v2)
*Kenneth J. K. Ong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究视觉提示对VLM合作行为影响，对agent决策模块设计有潜在启发。

Original abstract: As Vision-Language Models (VLMs) become increasingly integrated into decision-making systems, it is essential to understand how visual inputs influence their behavior. This paper investigates the effects of visual priming on VLMs' cooperative behavior using the Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma (IPD) as a test scenario. We examine whether exposure to images depicting behavioral concepts (kindness/helpfulness vs. aggressiveness/selfishness) and color-coded reward matrices alters VLM decision patterns. Experiments were conducted across multiple state-of-the-art VLMs. We further explore mitigation strategies including prompt modifications, Chain of Thought (CoT) reasoning, and visual token reduction. Results show that VLM behavior can be influenced by both image content and color cues, with varying susceptibility and mitigation effectiveness across models. These findings not only underscore the importance of robust evaluation frameworks for VLM deployment in visually rich and safety-critical environments, but also highlight how architectural and training differences among models may lead to distinct behavioral responses-an area worthy of further investigation.

Method: 提出了一个原则性分类法，将现有方法分为离线RL、在线RL和混合策略，并分析了奖励工程、数据效率和关键技术。

Result: 揭示了三个趋势：可靠性与可扩展性驱动复合奖励架构；GUI I/O延迟加速世界模型训练；系统2式思考自发涌现，表明丰富奖励信号可替代显式推理监督。

Original abstract: Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents have emerged as a promising paradigm for intelligent systems that perceive and interact with graphical interfaces visually. Yet supervised fine-tuning alone cannot handle long-horizon credit assignment, distribution shifts, and safe exploration in irreversible environments, making Reinforcement Learning (RL) a central methodology for advancing automation. In this work, we present the first comprehensive overview of the intersection between RL and GUI agents, and examine how this research direction may evolve toward digital inhabitants. We propose a principled taxonomy that organizes existing methods into Offline RL, Online RL, and Hybrid Strategies, and complement it with analyses of reward engineering, data efficiency, and key technical innovations. Our analysis reveals several emerging trends: the tension between reliability and scalability is motivating the adoption of composite, multi-tier reward architectures; GUI I/O latency bottlenecks are accelerating the shift toward world-model-based training, which can yield substantial performance gains; and the spontaneous emergence of System-2-style deliberation suggests that explicit reasoning supervision may not be necessary when sufficiently rich reward signals are available. We distill these findings into a roadmap covering process rewards, continual RL, cognitive architectures, and safe deployment, aiming to guide the next generation of robust GUI automation and its agent-native infrastructure.

### [60] [LLMs as ASP Programmers: Self-Correction Enables Task-Agnostic Nonmonotonic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27960v2)
*Adam Ishay,Joohyung Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM+ASP非单调推理框架含自我纠错，适用于agent逻辑推理与反馈循环。

TL;DR: 提出LLM+ASP框架，利用非单调逻辑和自动自我校正循环，无需领域工程，在非单调推理任务上显著优于SMT方法，并发现紧凑上下文指南优于冗长文档的“上下文腐烂”现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM存在高计算成本、逻辑不一致和高复杂度性能下降问题；神经符号方法依赖单调逻辑，无法处理可废止推理（人类认知的关键组成部分）。

Method: 提出LLM+ASP框架，将自然语言转化为基于稳定模型语义的回答集编程（ASP），利用自动自我校正循环从ASP求解器获取结构化反馈进行迭代细化，无需任何任务特定工程。

Result: 在六个基准上评估：（1）稳定模型语义在非单调任务上显著优于SMT；（2）迭代自我校正主要驱动性能，替代手工领域知识；（3）紧凑上下文参考指南优于冗长文档，揭示了“上下文腐烂”现象。

Conclusion: LLM+ASP框架有效实现非单调推理，减少人工干预，自我校正确保性能，同时紧凑上下文指南更优，为神经符号整合提供新方向。

中文摘要：近年来，大型语言模型（LLM）在推理方面取得了令人瞩目的里程碑，但仍面临高计算成本、逻辑不一致以及在高度复杂问题上性能急剧下降等问题。虽然神经符号方法试图通过将LLM与符号推理器耦合来缓解这些问题，但现有方法通常依赖于单调逻辑（例如SMT），这种逻辑无法表示可废止推理——这是人类认知的基本组成部分。我们提出了“LLM+ASP”框架，该框架将自然语言转化为回答集编程（ASP），一种基于稳定模型语义的非单调形式化方法。与先前需要手动编写知识模块、领域特定提示或评估仅限于单一问题类别的“LLM+ASP”方法不同，我们的框架无需任何针对特定任务的工程化处理，并且统一适用于多种推理任务。我们的系统利用一个自动自我校正循环，其中来自ASP求解器的结构化反馈能够进行迭代细化。通过对六个不同基准的评估，我们证明：（1）稳定模型语义允许LLM自然地表达默认规则和例外，在非单调任务上显著优于基于SMT的替代方案；（2）迭代自我校正是性能的主要驱动因素，有效取代了对手工领域知识的需求；（3）紧凑的上下文参考指南显著优于冗长的文档，揭示了一种“上下文腐烂”现象，即过多的上下文会妨碍约束遵循。

Original abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) have achieved impressive reasoning milestones but continue to struggle with high computational costs, logical inconsistencies, and sharp performance degradation on high-complexity problems. While neuro-symbolic methods attempt to mitigate these issues by coupling LLMs with symbolic reasoners, existing approaches typically rely on monotonic logics (e.g., SMT) that cannot represent defeasible reasoning -- essential components of human cognition. We present "LLM+ASP," a framework that translates natural language into Answer Set Programming (ASP), a nonmonotonic formalism based on stable model semantics. Unlike prior "LLM+ASP" approaches that require manually authored knowledge modules, domain-specific prompts, or evaluation restricted to single problem classes, our framework operates without any per-task engineering and applies uniformly across diverse reasoning tasks. Our system utilizes an automated self-correction loop where structured feedback from the ASP solver enables iterative refinement. Evaluating across six diverse benchmarks, we demonstrate that: (1) stable model semantics allow LLMs to naturally express default rules and exceptions, outperforming SMT-based alternatives by significant margins on nonmonotonic tasks; (2) iterative self-correction is the primary driver of performance, effectively replacing the need for handcrafted domain knowledge; (3) compact in-context reference guides substantially outperform verbose documentation, revealing a "context rot" phenomenon where excessive context hinders constraint adherence.

### [61] [Language Models Refine Mechanical Linkage Designs Through Symbolic Reflection and Modular Optimisation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27962v1)
*João Pedro Gandarela,Thiago Rios,Stefan Menzel,André Freitas*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent进行机械设计优化，符号抽象与迭代细化方法可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 语言模型通过符号抽象表示和数值优化迭代改进机械连杆设计，显著降低几何误差并提高结构有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机械连杆设计面临组合拓扑选择和连续参数拟合的挑战，现有方法难以兼顾，因此探索语言模型通过符号表示进行系统性改进。

Method: 语言模型代理探索离散拓扑，数值优化器拟合连续参数；符号提升算子将模拟轨迹转换为定性描述、运动标签、时间谓词和结构诊断，模型在迭代设计周期中利用这些信息进行改进。

Result: 在六个工程目标和三个开源模型上，模块化架构相比基线减少几何误差达68%，提高结构有效性达134%；78.6%的迭代轨迹有可测量改进，正确诊断过约束（56.3%）和欠约束（35.6%）故障模式。

Conclusion: 原则性的符号抽象能够弥合生成式AI与工程设计所需数值精度之间的差距，使语言模型无需微调即可获得可解释的机械推理策略。

中文摘要：设计机械连杆涉及组合拓扑选择和连续参数拟合。我们展示了语言模型可以通过符号表示系统地改进连杆设计。语言模型代理探索离散拓扑，而数值优化器拟合连续参数。符号提升算子将模拟器轨迹转换为定性描述、运动标签、时间谓词和结构诊断，模型在迭代设计周期中解释这些信息。在六个工程相关的运动目标和三个开源模型（Llama 3.3 70B、Qwen3 4B、Qwen3 MoE 30B-A3B）上，模块化架构相比单体基线减少了高达68%的几何误差，并提高了高达134%的结构有效性。关键的是，78.6%的迭代细化轨迹显示出可测量的改进，系统正确诊断了过约束（56.3%）和欠约束（35.6%）故障模式，并提出了基于实际的修正。三个模型家族的所有模型都在没有微调的情况下获得了可解释的机械推理策略，证明了原则性的符号抽象弥合了生成式AI和工程设计所需的数值精度。

Original abstract: Designing mechanical linkages involves combinatorial topology selection and continuous parameter fitting. We show that language models can systematically improve linkage designs through symbolic representations. Language model agents explore discrete topologies while numerical optimisers fit continuous parameters. A symbolic lifting operator translates simulator trajectories into qualitative descriptors, motion labels, temporal predicates, and structural diagnostics that models interpret across iterative design cycles. Across six engineering-relevant motion targets and three open-source models (Llama 3.3 70B, Qwen3 4B, Qwen3 MoE 30B-A3B), the modular architecture reduces geometric error by up to 68% and improves structural validity by up to 134% over monolithic baselines. Critically, 78.6% of iterative refinement trajectories show measurable improvement, with the system correctly diagnosing overconstraint (56.3%) and underconstraint (35.6%) failure modes and proposing grounded corrections. Models across all three families acquire interpretable mechanical reasoning strategies without fine-tuning, demonstrating that principled symbolic abstraction bridges generative AI and the numerical precision required for engineering design.

### [62] [D3-Gym: Constructing Real-World Verifiable Environments for Data-Driven Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27977v2)
*Hanane Nour Moussa,Yifei Li,Zhuoyang Li,Yankai Yang,Cheng Tang,Tianshu Zhang,Nesreen K. Ahmed,Ali Payani,Ziru Chen,Huan Sun*

TL;DR: D3-Gym是首个自动构建的、用于科学数据驱动发现的可验证环境数据集，包含565个来自真实科学代码仓库的任务，其评估脚本与人工黄金标准一致性达87.5%，并且基于其轨迹训练能显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: D3-Gym通过自动构建包含自然语言指令、可执行环境、数据集、参考代码和自动合成评估脚本的565个任务（来自239个真实科学代码仓库），并提供验证信号质量评估。

Result: 评估脚本与人工黄金标准一致性达87.5%；基于D3-Gym轨迹训练使Qwen3-32B在ScienceAgentBench上提升7.8个绝对百分点，缩小与专有模型的差距。

Conclusion: D3-Gym提供了可验证的科学数据驱动发现环境，其高质量验证信号和训练轨迹能有效提升模型性能，推动了该领域的发展。

中文摘要：尽管近期在用于科学数据驱动发现的语言模型和智能体方面取得了进展，但缺乏代表真实科学任务的可验证环境阻碍了其能力的进一步提升。为填补这一空白，我们引入了D3-Gym，这是首个自动构建的、包含可验证环境的科学数据驱动发现数据集。D3-Gym包含（1）来自四个学科239个真实科学代码仓库的565个任务，其中（2）每个任务都配有自然语言指令、预装依赖的可执行环境、输入数据集和工件预览、参考代码解决方案以及自动合成的评估脚本。对D3-Gym中验证信号质量的严格评估证实，我们的评估脚本与人工标注黄金标准的一致性达到87.5%，并且在领域特定评估逻辑上具有强对齐性，表明了其科学合理性。此外，在从D3-Gym采样的轨迹上进行训练，在ScienceAgentBench上对不同规模的Qwen3模型产生了持续且显著的性能提升，使Qwen3-32B提升了7.8个绝对百分点，并大幅缩小了与强专有模型之间的差距。所有D3-Gym工件（环境、创建流程、轨迹和模型）均可从https://github.com/OSU-NLP-Group/D3-Gym获取。

Original abstract: Despite recent progress in language models and agents for scientific data-driven discovery, further advancing their capabilities is held back by the absence of verifiable environments representing real-world scientific tasks. To fill this gap, we introduce D3-Gym, the first automatically constructed dataset with verifiable environments for scientific Data-Driven Discovery. D3-Gym comprises (1) 565 tasks sourced from 239 real scientific repositories across four disciplines where (2) each task is equipped with a natural language instruction, an executable environment with pre-installed dependencies, input dataset and artifact previews, a reference code solution, and an automatically synthesized evaluation script. Rigorous evaluation of the quality of the verification signal in D3-Gym confirms that our evaluation scripts achieve 87.5% agreement with human-annotated gold standards and strong alignment in domain-specific evaluation logic, showing their scientific soundness. Further, training on trajectories sampled from D3-Gym yields consistent and substantial gains across Qwen3 models of varying sizes on ScienceAgentBench, boosting Qwen3-32B by 7.8 absolute points and substantially shrinking the gap with strong proprietary models. All D3-Gym artifacts (environments, creation workflow, trajectories, and models) can be found at https://github.com/OSU-NLP-Group/D3-Gym.

### [63] [Exploring LLM Agent Designs and Interaction Modalities for Scientific Visualization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27996v3)
*Jackson Vonderhorst,Kuangshi Ai,Haichao Miao,Shusen Liu,Chaoli Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 系统比较多种LLM agent设计，对coding agent有借鉴

TL;DR: 本文比较了三种LLM智能体在科学可视化任务上的表现，发现通用编码智能体成功率最高但成本高，领域特定智能体高效但灵活性低，未来系统应结合结构化工具、交互和自适应记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对LLM智能体在科学可视化任务中不同设计和交互模式的系统性比较，需要明确其权衡以指导未来系统设计。

Method: 构建15个基准任务，对比三种智能体设计（领域特定、计算机使用、通用编码）和四种交互模式（代码脚本、MCP/API、CLI、GUI），评估可视化质量、效率、鲁棒性、计算成本和持久记忆影响。

Result: 通用编码智能体任务成功率最高但计算成本高；领域特定智能体更高效稳定但灵活性低；计算机使用智能体单步操作好但多步工作流差；持久记忆提升反复试验性能但依赖交互模式和反馈质量。

Conclusion: 未来SciVis系统应结合结构化工具使用、交互能力和自适应记忆机制以平衡性能、鲁棒性和灵活性。

中文摘要：本文研究了大语言模型（LLM）智能体在需要从自然语言指令生成可视化工作流的科学可视化（SciVis）任务上的表现。我们比较了三种代表性智能体设计：具有结构化工具使用的领域特定智能体、计算机使用智能体和通用编码智能体，在15个基准任务上评估了可视化质量、效率、鲁棒性、计算成本以及持久记忆的影响。我们进一步研究了交互模式，包括代码脚本、模型上下文协议（MCP）或API调用、命令行界面（CLI）和图形用户界面（GUI）。我们的目标是表征实践中使用的代表性SciVis智能体配置之间的权衡。结果揭示了智能体设计和交互模式之间的明确权衡。通用编码智能体实现了最高的任务成功率，但产生了更大的计算成本，而领域特定智能体更高效和稳定，但灵活性较低。计算机使用智能体在单个操作上表现良好，但在多步骤工作流上存在困难。在CLI和GUI设置中，持久记忆在重复试验中提高了性能，但其有效性取决于交互模式反馈的质量。这些发现表明，未来的SciVis系统应结合结构化工具使用、交互能力和自适应记忆机制，以平衡性能、鲁棒性和灵活性。

Original abstract: This paper examines how large language model (LLM) agents perform on scientific visualization (SciVis) tasks that require generating visualization workflows from natural-language instructions. We compare three representative agent designs: domain-specific agents with structured tool use, computer-use agents, and general-purpose coding agents, across 15 benchmark tasks, evaluating visualization quality, efficiency, robustness, computational cost, and the impact of persistent memory. We further study interaction modalities, including code scripts, model context protocol (MCP) or API calls, command-line interfaces (CLI), and graphical user interfaces (GUI). Our goal is to characterize the tradeoffs among representative SciVis agent configurations used in practice. The results reveal clear tradeoffs across agent designs and interaction modalities. General-purpose coding agents achieve the highest task success rates but incur greater computational cost, whereas domain-specific agents are more efficient and stable but less flexible. Computer-use agents perform well on individual operations but struggle with multi-step workflows. Across both CLI- and GUI-based settings, persistent memory improves performance over repeated trials, but its effectiveness depends on the interaction mode and the quality of feedback. These findings suggest that future SciVis systems should combine structured tool use, interactive capabilities, and adaptive memory mechanisms to balance performance, robustness, and flexibility.

</details>

Original abstract: Integrating multimodal foundation models into enterprise ecosystems presents a fundamental software architecture challenge. Architects must balance competing quality attributes: the high latency and non-determinism of vision language action (VLA) models versus the strict determinism and real-time performance required by enterprise control loops. In this study, we propose an architectural pattern language for visual agents that separates fast, deterministic reflexes from slow, probabilistic supervision. It consists of four architectural design patterns: (1) Hybrid Affordance Integration, (2) Adaptive Visual Anchoring, (3) Visual Hierarchy Synthesis, and (4) Semantic Scene Graph.
